### [1] [Synthetic Designed Experiments for Diagnosing Vision Model Failure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00832)
*Krisanu Sarkar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SDRS框架，将实验设计（DoE）统计理论引入合成数据生成，通过析因设计审计下游模型的因子敏感性，针对性生成数据修复两类失败模式，在多个视觉任务上验证有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前合成数据流水线以开环方式盲目采样，将合成数据视为廉价真实数据，未能诊断下游模型的实际需求，浪费了合成数据可独立控制场景因子的独特优势。

Method: 基于实验设计（DoE）统计理论，将下游模型视为黑箱系统、合成生成器视为实验装置，采用部分析因设计通过ANOVA分解审计模型的因子敏感性，将失败分为Type I（未覆盖）和Type II（虚假依赖）两类，后针对性生成数据修复。

Result: (1) dSprites诊断实验：审计正确识别两类缺口，靶向数据将准确率从49.9%提升至79.0%；(2) 过程场景密集分割：检测背景复杂度捷径，mIoU从0.948提升至0.998；(3) 纠缠检测实验：ANOVA审计能识别不完美生成器中的跨因子污染。

Conclusion: SDRS有效利用合成数据的可控性进行主动诊断与靶向修复；发现因子层面不变性惩罚可在因子间迁移敏感性，为表示层面修正提出一个开放问题。

Original Abstract: Current synthetic data pipelines for computer vision generate images without diagnosing what the downstream model actually needs. This open-loop paradigm treats synthetic data as cheap real data, randomly sampling the generator's output space and hoping to cover the model's failure modes. We argue this fundamentally misuses synthetic data's unique property: the controllable, independent variation of scene factors.Drawing on the statistical theory of Design of Experiments (DoE), we propose Synthetic Designed Experiments for Representational Sufficiency (SDRS). SDRS treats the downstream model as a black-box system and the synthetic generator as an experimental apparatus. Using fractional factorial designs, SDRS efficiently audits a model's factor-sensitivity profile via ANOVA decomposition. It classifies failures into two actionable types: Type I gaps (coverage failures on underrepresented factor levels) and Type II gaps (reliance on spurious nuisance dependencies). The audit then prescribes targeted synthetic data to address each gap type. We validate SDRS on three experiments: (1) a controlled diagnostic on dSprites with planted biases, where the audit correctly identifies both gap types and targeted data improves accuracy from 49.9% to 79.0%; (2) a dense segmentation task on procedural scenes, where detecting background-complexity shortcuts and applying targeted data improves mIoU from 0.948 to 0.998; and (3) an entanglement detection experiment showing that the ANOVA audit identifies cross-factor contamination in imperfect generators. Finally, we show that per-factor invariance penalties can transfer sensitivity between factors, identifying an open problem for representation-level correction.

中文摘要翻译: 当前的计算机视觉合成数据流水线在生成图像时，并未诊断下游模型的实际需求。这种开环范式将合成数据视为廉价的真实数据，随机采样生成器的输出空间，寄希望于覆盖模型的失败模式。我们认为这从根本上误用了合成数据的独特属性：场景因子的可控且独立变化。借鉴实验设计（DoE）的统计理论，我们提出了面向表示充分性的合成设计实验（SDRS）。SDRS将下游模型视为黑箱系统，将合成生成器视为实验装置。利用部分析因设计，SDRS通过ANOVA分解高效审计模型的因子敏感性剖面。它将失败分为两类可操作的缺口：Type I缺口（对未充分表示的因子水平的覆盖失败）和Type II缺口（对虚假的 nuisance 依赖的依赖）。审计随后针对每种缺口类型规定靶向合成数据。我们在三个实验上验证了SDRS：（1）在植入偏置的dSprites上进行受控诊断，审计正确识别了两种缺口类型，靶向数据将准确率从49.9%提升至79.0%；（2）在过程场景上的密集分割任务，检测到背景复杂度捷径并应用靶向数据后，mIoU从0.948提升至0.998；（3）纠缠检测实验表明，ANOVA审计能识别不完美生成器中的跨因子污染。最后，我们展示了因子层面的不变性惩罚可以在因子间迁移敏感性，指出了表示层面修正的一个开放问题。

</details>


### [2] [Single Image Defogging Using a Fourth-Order Telegraph PDE Guided by Physical Haze Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00878)
*Manish Kumar,Rajendra K. Ray*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种结合四阶非线性偏微分方程与物理雾形成模型的混合去雾方法，利用暗通道先验估计大气参数，通过四阶PDE演化实现图像恢复，在抑制雾霾的同时保持结构细节，实验结果表明该方法在视觉质量和结构保持方面表现良好。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现实场景中图像去雾是一个逆问题，由于场景深度未知、大气散射以及缺乏真实参考图像，现有方法存在局限性，需要一种能够有效抑制雾霾同时保持图像结构细节的去雾方法。

Method: 提出一种混合去雾模型，集成四阶非线性偏微分方程与物理雾形成模型。首先利用暗通道先验估计大气参数并生成引导图像，然后通过边自适应扩散系数和透射率加权的保真项，演化四阶telegraph型PDE进行最终恢复。采用相对误差范数准则判断收敛。

Result: 与暗通道先验、改进暗通道先验及基于变分的单图像去雾方法相比，该方法在有真实参考图像时使用MSE和SSIM进行定量评估，对真实雾图使用FADE、对比度恢复指数、平均梯度和熵等无参考指标进行评估。实验结果表明该方法能提供可比的视觉质量并保持结构细节。

Conclusion: 提出的混合PDE去雾方法能够有效抑制雾霾，保持图像结构细节，在视觉质量和定量指标上均表现良好。

Original Abstract: In real-world scenarios, image defogging is an inverse problem due to unknown scene depth, atmospheric scattering, and the common absence of ground truth . To resolve the issue, we propose a hybrid defogging model that integrates a fourth-order nonlinear PDE with a physical haze formation model. We used Dark Channel Prior to estimate atmospheric parameters and to generate a guidance image, while the final restoration is performed via a fourth-order PDE-based evolution. A fourth-order PDE of the type telegraph is then evolved, incorporating an edge-adaptive diffusion coefficient and a fidelity term weighted by the transmission map. Fourth-order diffusion effectively suppresses haze while preserving structural details, and the hyperbolic formulation improves numerical stability and convergence behavior. We use relative error norm criteria for the convergence of our PDE. The proposed method is compared with Dark Channel prior, modified Dark Channel prior, and variational-based single-image defogging techniques. When we have ground truth available, we use MSE and SSIM for quantitative evaluation, whereas no-reference metrics, including FADE, Contrast Restoration Index, Average Gradient, and Entropy, are applied to real-world foggy images. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed hybrid PDE-based method provides comparable visual quality and maintains structural details.

中文摘要翻译: 在现实场景中，由于场景深度未知、大气散射以及通常缺乏真实参考图像，图像去雾是一个逆问题。为了解决这一问题，我们提出了一种混合去雾模型，该模型将四阶非线性偏微分方程与物理雾形成模型相结合。我们利用暗通道先验来估计大气参数并生成引导图像，而最终的恢复则通过基于四阶偏微分方程的演化来完成。随后，我们演化一种telegraph类型的四阶偏微分方程，其中包含边自适应扩散系数和由透射率加权的保真项。四阶扩散能有效抑制雾霾，同时保持结构细节，双曲型公式则改善了数值稳定性和收敛行为。我们使用相对误差范数准则来判断PDE的收敛。所提出的方法与暗通道先验、改进的暗通道先验以及基于变分的单图像去雾技术进行了比较。当有真实参考图像可用时，我们使用MSE和SSIM进行定量评估；而对于真实雾图，则采用包括FADE、对比度恢复指数、平均梯度和熵在内的无参考指标。实验结果表明，所提出的混合PDE方法能提供可比的视觉质量并保持结构细节。

</details>


### [3] [Intervention-Based Self-Supervised Learning: A Causal Probe Paradigm for Remote Photoplethysmography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00882)
*Zhiyi Niu,Xiaoguang Tu,Bo Zhao,Junzhe Cao,Dan Guo,Zitong Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出生理因果探测（PCP）新范式，通过主动干预视频色度分量来验证rPPG信号的物理真实性，从而避免自监督学习中常见的相关性陷阱，显著提升了跨域泛化性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有自监督rPPG方法容易陷入相关性陷阱：模型倾向于学习数据中最显著的周期信号（如高能运动或光照噪声），而非微弱的真实rPPG信号，导致泛化能力差。

Method: 提出PCP范式及Interv-rPPG框架：(1) PhysMambaFormer作为rPPG提取器提出rPPG假设信号；(2) 可控生理信号编辑器基于该假设对视频低频谱色度分量进行精确干预；(3) 通过"归零可证伪性"和"公理等变性"验证假设的物理真实性。

Result: 在VIPL-HR和MMPD等挑战性数据集上，域内和跨域性能均显著提升；在复杂跨数据集设置中超越有监督基线；在干净数据集中仍具竞争力（干预机制可能引入轻微残留色度噪声）。消融实验表明PCP范式有效抵抗运动和光照伪影。

Conclusion: PCP范式通过从被动相关性学习转向主动因果干预，有效解决了rPPG自监督学习中的相关性陷阱问题，在抗干扰和泛化能力上均优于现有方法。

Original Abstract: Remote Photoplethysmography (rPPG) enables convenient non-contact physiological measurement. Existing Self-Supervised Learning (SSL) methods commonly fall into a correlation trap: they tend to learn the most dominant periodic signals in the data, such as high-energy motion or illumination noise, rather than the faint, true rPPG signal, leading to poor model generalization. To address this, we propose a new SSL paradigm, Physiological Causal Probing (PCP), which treats the latent rPPG signal as the underlying physical source and the resulting pixel chrominance variations as its visual manifestation. Its core idea is to shift from passive correlation learning to active, precise intervention: it intervenes on the video based on a proposed rPPG hypothesis, and verifies whether the post-intervention changes match physical expectations. We propose the Interv-rPPG framework to implement PCP: an rPPG extractor named PhysMambaFormer hypothesizes the rPPG signal, while a Controllable Physiological Signal Editor conducts precise chrominance-domain interventions on videos based on this hypothesis. Interv-rPPG validates the physical realism of the hypothesis through `Falsifiability via Nulling' and `Axiomatic Equivariance'. Our editor achieves precise editing of the rPPG signal by intervening in the low-frequency chrominance components of the video. Our method improves both in-domain and cross-domain performance on challenging datasets such as VIPL-HR and MMPD. Furthermore, it surpasses the supervised baseline in complex cross-dataset settings, while remaining competitive on clean datasets where the intervention mechanism may introduce slight residual chrominance noise. Extensive experiments, including diagnostic analysis of nuisance sensitivity, demonstrate that the PCP paradigm effectively resists motion and illumination artifacts.

中文摘要翻译: 远程光电容积描记术（rPPG）能够实现便捷的非接触式生理测量。现有的自监督学习（SSL）方法通常陷入相关性陷阱：它们倾向于学习数据中最显著的周期信号，例如高能运动或光照噪声，而非微弱的真实rPPG信号，导致模型泛化能力差。为解决这一问题，我们提出了一种新的自监督学习范式——生理因果探测（PCP），该范式将潜在rPPG信号视为底层物理源，将由此产生的像素色度变化视为其视觉表现。其核心思想是从被动的相关性学习转向主动的、精确的干预：它基于提出的rPPG假设对视频进行干预，并验证干预后的变化是否符合物理预期。我们提出了Interv-rPPG框架来实现PCP：一个名为PhysMambaFormer的rPPG提取器提出rPPG假设，同时一个可控生理信号编辑器基于该假设对视频进行精确的色度域干预。Interv-rPPG通过"归零可证伪性"和"公理等变性"验证假设的物理真实性。我们的编辑器通过干预视频的低频谱色度分量实现了对rPPG信号的精确编辑。该方法在VIPL-HR和MMPD等具有挑战性的数据集上同时提升了域内和跨域性能。此外，它在复杂的跨数据集设置中超越了有监督基线，同时在干净数据集上保持竞争力（尽管干预机制可能引入轻微的残留色度噪声）。大量实验（包括对干扰敏感性的诊断分析）表明，PCP范式能够有效抵抗运动和光照伪影。

</details>


### [4] [LiteVLA-H: Dual-Rate Vision-Language-Action Inference for Onboard Aerial Guidance and Semantic Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00884)
*Justn williams,Kishor Datta Gupta,Roy George,Mrinmoy Sarkar*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LiteVLA-H是一个紧凑的256M参数视觉-语言-动作模型，专为无人机边缘部署设计，在NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin上实现双速率运行：快速外环制导（19.74Hz）和慢速语义模式（6-7Hz），通过调度器利用多模态预填充主导延迟的特性，实现低延迟闭环制导与周期性语义感知的兼顾。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有VLA模型在语义基础与任务泛化上表现良好，但空中部署面临严格的计算和通信约束，需要低延迟闭环制导；同时紧凑边缘设备上的端到端延迟主要由多模态预填充主导，而非解码额外token的边际成本，这为设计双速率调度策略提供了契机。

Method: 提出LiteVLA-H紧凑型256M参数VLA系统，在NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin上运行；设计调度器以双速率模式工作：快速外环制导输出短动作token（50.65ms/19.74Hz），慢速语义模式输出句子级语义（149.90-164.57ms/6-7Hz）；采用知识保留微调策略，混合反应式飞行数据、空中语义数据和通用描述/VQA监督，避免模型描述能力崩溃。

Result: 动作分支在边缘推理速率上达到19.74Hz（50.65ms），语义模式达到6.08-6.67Hz（149.90-164.57ms）；与AnywhereVLA、FutureVLA、ReMem-VLA等最新架构相比，在部署条件下动作分支实现了更高的边缘推理速率，同时保留周期性语义感知能力。

Conclusion: LiteVLA-H在紧凑边缘设备上实现了低延迟空中闭环制导与语义理解的平衡，验证了多模态预填充主导延迟的观察，双速率调度策略和知识保留微调方法对边缘VLA部署具有实用价值。

Original Abstract: Vision-language-action (VLA) models have shown strong semantic grounding and task generalization in manipulation, but aerial deployment remains difficult because drones require low-latency closed-loop guidance under strict onboard compute and communication constraints. We present LiteVLA-H, a compact 256M-parameter VLA system designed for dual-rate operation on an NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin: a fast outer-loop guidance mode for short action-token outputs and a slower semantic mode for scene understanding, hazard description, and operator-facing narration. The central empirical observation is that, in this compact edge regime, end-to-end latency is dominated by multimodal pre-fill rather than by the marginal cost of decoding a few extra tokens. This motivates a scheduler that issues reactive action tokens at 50.65,ms (19.74,Hz) while still supporting sentence-level semantic outputs at 149.90--164.57\ms (6.08--6.67,Hz) on the same embedded platform. To specialize the model without collapsing its descriptive competence, we use a knowledge-preserving fine-tuning recipe that mixes reactive flight data, aerial semantic data, and generic caption/VQA supervision. Beyond reporting current latency measurements, we position the system against recent state-of-the-art architectures, including AnywhereVLA, FutureVLA, and ReMem-VLA, showing that the measured action branch reaches a higher edge inference rate under our deployment conditions while retaining periodic semantic awareness.

中文摘要翻译: 视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在操作任务中展现出强大的语义基础与任务泛化能力，但空中部署仍面临挑战，因为无人机需要在严格机载计算和通信约束下实现低延迟闭环制导。我们提出LiteVLA-H，一个紧凑的256M参数VLA系统，专为NVIDIA Jetson AGX Orin上的双速率运行设计：快速外环制导模式用于短动作token输出，以及较慢的语义模式用于场景理解、危险描述和面向操作员的叙述。核心实证观察是，在这种紧凑边缘场景中，端到端延迟主要由多模态预填充主导，而非解码少量额外token的边际成本。这一观察启发我们设计调度器，使其在同一嵌入式平台上能以50.65ms（19.74Hz）输出反应式动作token，同时仍支持149.90-164.57ms（6.08-6.67Hz）的句子级语义输出。为避免模型描述能力崩溃的同时实现专业化，我们采用知识保留微调策略，混合反应式飞行数据、空中语义数据以及通用描述/VQA监督。除报告当前的延迟测量结果外，我们将系统与包括AnywhereVLA、FutureVLA和ReMem-VLA在内的最新先进架构进行对比，表明在我们的部署条件下，所测得的动作分支在保留周期性语义感知能力的同时，达到了更高的边缘推理速率。

</details>


### [5] [Quantum Gradient-Based Approach for Edge and Corner Detection Using Sobel Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00744)
*Mohammad Aamir Sohail,Gabriela Pinheiro,Yasemin Poyraz Kocak,Batuhan Hangun,Emre Camkerten,Simge Yigit,Hafize Asude Ertan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于量子的Sobel边缘检测和Harris角点检测实现方法，比较了FRQI和QPIE两种量子图像编码方式，引入基于lag-2差分的高效梯度计算方案，并辅以经典后处理提升检测质量。实验表明量子电路输出与经典方法一致，QPIE在有限测量下更稳定，但整体成本仍由态制备、测量和后处理主导。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 探索边缘检测和角点检测在量子计算框架下的可行实现方案，对比不同量子图像编码方法的性能，为量子图像处理提供功能验证和可扩展的量子-经典混合计算路径。

Method: 使用FRQI和QPIE两种量子图像编码方法；提出基于lag-2差分的量子梯度计算方案，在叠加态中高效评估类梯度特征；对量子电路识别的候选角点施加经典后处理步骤以减少误检。

Result: 量子电路输出与经典Sobel和Harris算子结果一致；QPIE方案在有限测量次数下比FRQI更稳定、更连贯；梯度计算在电路层面高效，但整体开销仍由态制备、测量和经典后处理主导。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种功能完整且可扩展的经典边缘和角点检测方法的量子实现，而非端到端的加速方案；在无噪声仿真下验证了可行性，但NISQ硬件上的性能可能受噪声和测量限制影响。

Original Abstract: Edge detection refers to identifying points in a digital image where intensity changes sharply, indicating object boundaries or structural features. Corners are locations where gray-level intensity changes abruptly in multiple directions and are widely used in feature extraction, object tracking, and 3D modeling. In this study, we present a quantum implementation of Sobel-based edge detection and Harris-style corner detection. Two quantum image encoding methods - Flexible Representation of Quantum Images (FRQI) and Quantum Probability Image Encoding (QPIE) - are used to encode the input data and are comparatively analyzed. The proposed approach introduces a quantum gradient computation scheme based on lag-2 differences, enabling the evaluation of gradient-like features in superposition. To improve detection quality and reduce false positives, a classical post-processing step is applied to candidate corner points identified by the quantum circuit. Results show that the proposed quantum circuits produce outputs consistent with classical Sobel and Harris operators. Furthermore, the QPIE-based configuration yields more stable and coherent results than FRQI, especially under limited measurement shots. While gradient computation can be performed efficiently at the circuit level, the overall cost remains dominated by state preparation, measurement, and classical post-processing. All experiments are conducted under noiseless simulation, and performance on NISQ hardware may be affected by noise and measurement limitations. Therefore, this work demonstrates a functional and scalable quantum realization of classical edge and corner detection methods rather than an end-to-end speedup.

中文摘要翻译: 边缘检测是指在数字图像中识别亮度发生剧烈变化的点，这些点通常对应物体边界或结构特征。角点是灰度强度在多个方向上发生突变的像素位置，广泛应用于特征提取、目标跟踪和三维建模。在本研究中，我们提出了一种基于量子的Sobel边缘检测和Harris角点检测实现方案。采用两种量子图像编码方法——量子图像的灵活表示（FRQI）和量子概率图像编码（QPIE）——对输入数据进行编码，并进行了对比分析。所提出的方法引入了一种基于lag-2差分的量子梯度计算方案，能够在叠加态中高效评估类梯度特征。为提升检测质量并减少误检，对量子电路识别的候选角点施加了经典后处理步骤。结果表明，所提出的量子电路输出与经典Sobel和Harris算子的结果一致。此外，基于QPIE的配置在有限测量次数下比FRQI产生更稳定和连贯的结果。尽管梯度计算在电路层面可以高效执行，但整体成本仍由态制备、测量和经典后处理主导。所有实验均在无噪声仿真环境下进行，在NISQ硬件上的性能可能受到噪声和测量限制的影响。因此，本工作展示的是一种功能完整且可扩展的经典边缘和角点检测方法的量子实现，而非端到端的加速方案。

</details>


### [6] [Selective Correlation Based Knowledge Distillation for Ground Reaction Force Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00888)
*Eun Som Jeon,Jisoo Lee,Huisu Lim,Omik M. Save,Hyunglae Lee,Pavan Turaga*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出选择性相关性知识蒸馏（SCKD）方法，从穿戴式鞋垫传感器数据中估计地面反作用力（GRF），在保持高精度的同时降低计算资源需求，实现便携式步态分析。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统GRF测量依赖实验室测力台，设备昂贵且不便携；穿戴式鞋垫传感器虽便携但易受噪声干扰导致测量精度低；深度学习方法虽可提升精度但计算开销大，难以在便携设备上实现实时分析。

Method: 提出选择性相关性知识蒸馏（SCKD）框架，利用时间特征选择关键特征提取相关性图进行知识迁移，将大型教师模型的知识蒸馏到紧凑的学生模型中，在降低计算复杂度的同时保持高精度。

Result: 在不同步行速度和窗口大小配置下，通过多种评价标准对比，SCKD生成的紧凑模型在从穿戴式鞋垫传感器数据估计GRF方面优于现有方法。

Conclusion: SCKD方法为基于穿戴式传感器的步态分析提供了可靠且资源高效的解决方案，在保证估计精度的同时显著降低了计算资源需求，适用于便携式实时分析场景。

Original Abstract: Wearable sensor-based human gait analysis holds great promise in healthcare, rehabilitation, clinical diagnosis and monitoring, and sports activities. Specifically, ground reaction force (GRF) provides essential insights into the body's interaction with the ground during movement and is typically measured using instrumented treadmills equipped with force plates. However, such equipment is expensive and restricted to laboratory environments. To enable a more portable solution, wearable insole sensors have been used to measure GRF. These sensors, however, are prone to noise and external interference, which reduces measurement accuracy. Deep learning methodologies could be adopted to address these issues, but they often require significant computing resources to achieve high accuracy, limiting their applicability for real-time analysis on portable devices. To overcome these limitations, we propose Selective Correlation Based Knowledge Distillation (SCKD) for estimating GRF from data collected by insole sensors. Our proposed method utilizes selected features considering temporal characteristics in the process of extracting correlation maps for knowledge transfer, enhancing interpretability and mitigating issues in high dimensional data processing. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the compact models generated by our distillation framework through comparison with existing methods. Various configurations of teacher-student architectures and training approaches are examined based on multiple evaluation criteria, utilizing data collected at different walking speeds and with different window sizes. Experimental results confirm that our approach outperforms existing methods in estimating GRF from wearable insole sensor data. Therefore, our approach offers a reliable and resource-efficient solution for human gait analysis.

中文摘要翻译: 基于可穿戴传感器的步态分析在医疗保健、康复、临床诊断与监测以及体育活动中具有广阔前景。具体而言，地面反作用力（GRF）能提供运动过程中身体与地面相互作用的重要信息，通常使用配备测力板的仪器化跑步机进行测量。然而，此类设备成本高昂且局限于实验室环境。为实现更具便携性的解决方案，研究者使用可穿戴鞋垫传感器来测量GRF。但这些传感器易受噪声和外部干扰影响，导致测量精度下降。深度学习方法虽可用于解决这些问题，但为实现高精度往往需要大量计算资源，限制了其在便携设备上进行实时分析的适用性。为克服上述局限性，我们提出了一种基于选择性相关性的知识蒸馏（SCKD）方法，用于从鞋垫传感器采集的数据中估计GRF。该方法在提取相关性图以进行知识迁移的过程中，利用时间特征选择关键特征，增强了可解释性并缓解了高维数据处理中的问题。通过与现有方法的比较，我们验证了蒸馏框架生成的紧凑模型的有效性。基于在不同步行速度和不同窗口大小下采集的数据，我们根据多种评价标准考察了多种师生架构配置及训练方法。实验结果证实，我们的方法在从可穿戴鞋垫传感器数据估计GRF方面优于现有方法。因此，本方法为人体步态分析提供了一种可靠且资源高效的解决方案。

### [7] [SparseContrast: Dynamic Sparse Attention for Efficient and Accurate Contrastive Learning in Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00887)
*Paarth Prasad,Ruchika Malhotra*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出SparseContrast框架，融合动态稀疏注意力与对比学习，用于低数据量下的胸部X光疾病检测，在保持诊断精度的同时将训练和推理速度提升高达40%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统对比学习依赖密集注意力机制，计算开销大且处理医学图像中的冗余区域；低数据量场景下需要兼顾计算效率与诊断准确性。

Method: 引入稀疏注意力机制，通过紧凑的显著性预测器在训练阶段自适应修剪注意力图，同时优化稀疏性和特征质量，实现对诊断相关区域的选择性聚焦。

Result: 相比密集注意力基线，训练和推理速度提升高达40%；在疾病识别任务上达到与现有方法相当或更优的性能；该方法对骨干架构无偏好，可应用于卷积和Transformer模型。

Conclusion: SparseContrast为资源受限的医学影像场景提供了一种实用的对比学习方案，有效平衡了计算效率与诊断精度，且具有良好的架构通用性。

Original Abstract: We propose SparseContrast, a new framework that merges dynamic sparse attention with contrastive learning for medical imaging, with a focus on chest X-ray disease detection in low-data settings. Traditional contrastive learning methods rely on dense attention mechanisms, which are computationally expensive and often process redundant regions in medical images. To resolve this, SparseContrast introduces a sparse attention mechanism that selectively concentrates on diagnostically pertinent areas, markedly decreasing computational burden without compromising accuracy. The framework adaptively trims attention maps in the training phase, directed by a compact saliency predictor which concurrently optimizes sparsity and feature quality. This method not only speeds up training and inference by as much as 40% relative to dense attention benchmarks but also boosts diagnostic accuracy by focusing on areas of clinical importance. Moreover, the approach remains indifferent to the selection of backbone architecture, which permits its application to both convolutional and transformer-based models. Experiments show SparseContrast attains comparable or better performance in disease identification tasks with greater efficiency relative to current approaches. The proposed framework delivers a practical approach for implementing contrastive learning in medical imaging settings with limited resources, where computational efficiency and diagnostic accuracy are paramount.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了SparseContrast，一种将动态稀疏注意力与对比学习相结合的新框架，专注于低数据量场景下的胸部X光疾病检测。传统的对比学习方法依赖密集注意力机制，计算开销大且常处理医学图像中的冗余区域。为解决这一问题，SparseContrast引入了一种稀疏注意力机制，选择性地聚焦于诊断相关区域，在不牺牲精度的前提下显著降低计算负担。该框架在训练阶段自适应地修剪注意力图，由紧凑的显著性预测器引导，同时优化稀疏性和特征质量。该方法不仅相比密集注意力基线将训练和推理速度提升高达40%，还通过聚焦临床重要区域提升了诊断准确性。此外，该方法对骨干架构的选择具有无关性，可应用于卷积模型和基于Transformer的模型。实验表明，SparseContrast在疾病识别任务上以更高效率达到了与现有方法相当或更优的性能。该框架为资源有限的医学影像场景提供了一种实用的对比学习方法，在这些场景中，计算效率和诊断准确性至关重要。

### [8] [GameScope: A Multi-Attribute, Multi-Codec Benchmark Dataset for Gaming Video Quality Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01272)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有游戏视频质量评估数据集数量有限且各有局限，缺乏覆盖多种编码器（H.264、H.265、AV1）和多种内容类型（UGC和PGC）的大规模、多样化数据集，无法支持跨编码器一致工作的质量评估模型。

Method: 构建了包含4,048个视频样本的大型游戏视频质量数据集，覆盖H.264、H.265和AV1三种主流编码器，包含用户生成内容（UGC）和专业生成内容（PGC），每个样本由平均37人标注平均意见得分（MOS），并收集了粗粒度的质量属性。

Result: 在数据集上评估了领先的视频质量评估方法，其中视觉语言模型（VLM）在所有基准方法中表现最佳；这是首个跨多种编码器和内容类型、包含质量属性的游戏视频质量评估数据集。

Conclusion: 该数据集填补了多编码器游戏视频质量评估的数据空白，为开发跨编码器一致工作的质量评估模型提供了基础，且已公开可供研究使用。

Original Abstract: The development of video game streaming has grown rapidly, with major platforms such as YouTube and Twitch using different codecs. To support quality assessment models that work consistently across any codec, it is necessary to have access to large, diverse subjective gaming quality datasets. Currently, there are only a few available, each having limitations. To address this gap, we present the largest gaming video quality dataset to date, incorporating both user-generated content (UGC) and professional-generated content (PGC) with extensive visual diversity. Our dataset covers the most widely used codecs - H.264, H.265, and AV1 - and consists of 4,048 video samples, each annotated by an average of 37 mean opinion score (MOS) ratings. In addition to overall quality scores, we collect coarse-grained quality attributes, enabling a better understanding of perceptual factors. We study the performance of leading video quality assessment methods on this dataset, including a vision language model that outperforms all the benchmarks. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first dataset that comprehensively addresses gaming video quality assessment across multiple codecs and content types with quality attributes. Our dataset is publicly available at https://rajeshsureddi.github.io/GameScope/.

### [9] [X2SAM: Any Segmentation in Images and Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00891)
*Hao Wang,Limeng Qiao,Chi Zhang,Lin Ma,Guanglu Wan,Xiangyuan Lan,Xiaodan Liang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: X2SAM是一个统一的分割多模态大语言模型，通过引入Mask Memory模块和联合训练策略，将任何分割能力从图像扩展到视频，支持多种分割任务和视觉/文本提示，同时保持图像和视频对话能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有MLLM缺乏像素级感知能力，SAM系列依赖低级视觉提示无法理解复杂指令，而现有的分割MLLM通常仅针对图像或视频单一模态设计，且很少在同一界面中同时支持文本和视觉提示，缺乏统一的图像-视频分割模型。

Method: X2SAM将LLM与Mask Memory模块耦合，该模块存储引导的视觉特征以实现时间上一致的视频掩码生成。采用统一的联合训练策略，在异构图像和视频数据集上训练，支持通用、开放词汇、指代、推理、接地对话生成、交互式和视觉接地分割等多种任务。

Result: X2SAM在视频分割任务上表现强劲，在图像分割基准上保持竞争力，同时保留了通用的图像和视频对话能力。此外，提出了Video Visual Grounded (V-VGD)分割基准用于评估模型从交互式视觉提示中分割视频中物体轨迹的能力。

Conclusion: X2SAM成功实现了从图像到视频的统一分割能力，通过一个统一的框架同时支持多种分割任务和两种模态，证明了联合训练策略的有效性以及Mask Memory模块在时间一致性视频掩码生成中的关键作用。

Original Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated strong image-level visual understanding and reasoning, yet their pixel-level perception across both images and videos remains limited. Foundation segmentation models such as the SAM series produce high-quality masks, but they rely on low-level visual prompts and cannot natively interpret complex conversational instructions. Existing segmentation MLLMs narrow this gap, but are usually specialized for either images or videos and rarely support both textual and visual prompts in one interface. We introduce X2SAM, a unified segmentation MLLM that extends any-segmentation capabilities from images to videos. Given conversational instructions and visual prompts, X2SAM couples an LLM with a Mask Memory module that stores guided vision features for temporally consistent video mask generation. The same formulation supports generic, open-vocabulary, referring, reasoning, grounded conversation generation, interactive, and visual grounded segmentation across image and video inputs. We further introduce the Video Visual Grounded (V-VGD) segmentation benchmark, which evaluates whether a model can segment object tracks in videos from interactive visual prompts. With a unified joint training strategy over heterogeneous image and video datasets, X2SAM delivers strong video segmentation performance, remains competitive on image segmentation benchmarks, and preserves general image and video chat ability.

中文摘要翻译: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在图像级别的视觉理解和推理方面表现出色，但其在图像和视频中的像素级感知能力仍然有限。SAM系列等基础分割模型能够生成高质量掩码，但它们依赖低级视觉提示，无法原生理解复杂的对话指令。现有的分割MLLMs缩小了这一差距，但通常专门针对图像或视频，且很少在同一界面中同时支持文本和视觉提示。我们提出了X2SAM，一个统一的分割多模态大语言模型，将任意分割能力从图像扩展到视频。给定对话指令和视觉提示，X2SAM将LLM与掩码记忆（Mask Memory）模块耦合，该模块存储引导的视觉特征，用于生成时间一致的视频掩码。相同的公式支持对图像和视频输入的通用分割、开放词汇分割、指代分割、推理分割、接地对话生成分割、交互式分割和视觉接地分割。我们还引入了视频视觉接地（Video Visual Grounded, V-VGD）分割基准，用于评估模型是否能够根据交互式视觉提示在视频中分割物体轨迹。通过在异构图像和视频数据集上的统一联合训练策略，X2SAM实现了强劲的视频分割性能，在图像分割基准上保持竞争力，并保留了通用的图像和视频对话能力。

### [10] [When To Adapt? Adapting the Model or Data in Federated Medical Imaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00892)
*Chamani Shiranthika,Parvaneh Saeedi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了联邦医学影像中两种主流领域自适应策略——数据层协调（Harmonization）和模型层个性化（Personalization），发现其效果取决于域偏移类型：外观变化时协调更优，结构差异时个性化更优，两者在客户端差异较小时效果相当。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 联邦学习在医学影像中常受客户端间域异质性影响，现有方法分为模型侧个性化和数据侧协调两大范式，但缺乏系统比较，导致实际应用中选择策略缺乏指导。

Method: 在六种医学影像场景（结肠息肉、皮肤病变、乳腺肿瘤分割，以及结核病CXR、脑肿瘤、乳腺肿瘤分类）下，覆盖多种域偏移类型，基于统一框架评估多种最先进的协调与个性化方法，比较其性能。

Result: 协调方法在外观变化主导的场景（如CXR分类）更有效；个性化方法在结构差异主导的场景（如结肠息肉分割）更有效；当客户端间差异较小时两者性能接近。存在条件性权衡关系。

Conclusion: 联邦医学影像中自适应策略的有效性取决于域偏移的类型和程度，而非单一策略。研究为选择协调或个性化提供了实用指南，并指出了未来混合方法的可行方向。

Original Abstract: Federated learning enables collaborative model training across medical institutions without sharing raw data, but its performance is often limited by domain heterogeneity across clients. Existing approaches to address this challenge fall into two main paradigms: model-side personalization, which adapts model parameters to each client, and data-side harmonization, which reduces inter-client variation at the input level. Despite their widespread use, these strategies have not been systematically compared. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive study across six medical imaging settings-colon polyp, skin lesion, and breast tumor segmentation, and tuberculosis CXR, brain tumor, and breast tumor classification-covering diverse types of domain shift. We evaluate a broad set of state-of-the-art harmonization and personalization methods under a unified framework. Our results reveal a conditional trade-off driven by the nature of heterogeneity: harmonization is more effective when variation is primarily appearance-based (e.g., CXR classification), while personalization performs better when differences are structural (e.g., colon polyp segmentation). When inter-client variation is limited, both strategies perform similarly. These findings demonstrate that the effectiveness of adaptation in federated medical imaging depends on the type and magnitude of domain shift rather than the strategy alone. We provide practical guidelines for selecting between harmonization and personalization and highlight directions for future hybrid approaches that combine both paradigms. Code is available at https://github.com/ChamaniS/WhenToAdapt.

中文摘要翻译: 联邦学习使得医疗机构无需共享原始数据即可进行协作模型训练，但其性能常常受到客户端间域异质性的限制。解决这一挑战的现有方法主要分为两种范式：模型侧个性化（model-side personalization），即为每个客户端适配模型参数；以及数据侧协调（data-side harmonization），即在输入层面减少客户端间的变异。尽管这两种策略被广泛使用，但它们尚未被系统性地比较。在本工作中，我们针对六种医学影像场景——结肠息肉、皮肤病变和乳腺肿瘤分割，以及结核病胸部X光、脑肿瘤和乳腺肿瘤分类——开展了全面的研究，覆盖了多种类型的域偏移。我们在统一框架下评估了一系列最先进的协调和个性化方法。结果显示存在一种由异质性性质决定的条件性权衡：当变异主要表现为外观层面时（如胸部X光分类），协调方法更为有效；而当差异体现在结构层面时（如结肠息肉分割），个性化方法表现更优。当客户端间变异有限时，两种策略表现相似。这些发现表明，联邦医学影像中自适应策略的有效性取决于域偏移的类型和程度，而非单一策略本身。我们为在协调与个性化之间进行选择提供了实用指南，并指出了未来结合两种范式的混合方法的方向。代码已开源：https://github.com/ChamaniS/WhenToAdapt。

</details>


### [11] [Retrieval-Guided Generation for Safer Histopathology Image Captioning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00893)
*Md. Enamul Hoq,Wataru Uegami,Saghir Alfasly,Ghazal Alabtah,Sahar Rahimi Malakshan,Armita Kazemi,Alex T. Schmitgen,Fred Prior,H. R. Tizhoosh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出检索引导生成（RGG）作为医学图像描述的安全替代方案，通过在ARCH组织病理学数据集上汇总相似案例的专家文本生成描述，相比完全生成式模型（如MedGemma）显著提升了语义对齐度（余弦相似度0.60 vs 0.47），并减少了幻觉和错误诊断，同时识别了概念混合等失败模式。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 生成式视觉-语言模型在生成流畅的医学图像描述时容易产生幻觉、过度具体的诊断声明和事实不一致的问题，这在病理学领域尤为严重，需要更可靠和可审计的替代方案。

Method: 采用检索引导生成（RGG）方法，不直接生成描述，而是从视觉相似的病例中检索专家文本并进行汇总，形成最终图像描述。

Result: 在ARCH组织病理学数据集上，RGG的语义对齐余弦相似度约为0.60，远高于MedGemma的约0.47，且置信区间不重叠。病理学家定性评审显示，RGG更好地保留了形态学相关术语，减少了无依据的诊断，但也发现了概念混合和继承过度标签等失败模式。

Conclusion: 检索引导的图像描述相比完全生成式方法提供了一种更透明、更可靠且更易于审计的医学图像描述方案。

Original Abstract: Generative vision-language models can produce fluent medical image captions but remain prone to hallucination, over-specific diagnostic claims, and factual inconsistency-serious issues in pathology. We investigate retrieval-guided generation (RGG) as a safer alternative, where captions are formed by summarizing expert text from visually similar cases rather than generated de novo. On the ARCH histopathology dataset, RGG improves semantic alignment with ground truth, achieving cosine similarity of $\approx$0.60 versus $\approx$0.47 from MedGemma, with non-overlapping confidence intervals indicating a robust gain. A pathologist-led qualitative review shows better preservation of morphology-relevant terminology and fewer unsupported diagnoses, while revealing failure modes such as concept mixing and inherited over-specific labeling. Overall, retrieval-guided captioning offers a more transparent and reliable approach with clearer opportunities for auditing than fully generative methods.

中文摘要翻译: 生成式视觉-语言模型能够生成流畅的医学图像描述，但仍容易出现幻觉、过度具体的诊断声明以及事实不一致的问题——这些在病理学领域尤为严重。我们研究了检索引导生成（RGG）作为一种更安全的替代方案，即通过汇总视觉相似病例中的专家文本来形成描述，而非从头开始生成。在ARCH组织病理学数据集上，RGG提高了与真实标注的语义对齐程度，余弦相似度约为0.60，而MedGemma约为0.47，且置信区间不重叠，表明取得了稳健的提升。病理学家主导的定性评审显示，RGG更好地保留了形态学相关术语，并减少了无依据的诊断，同时揭示了概念混合和继承过度标签等失败模式。总体而言，检索引导的图像描述提供了一种比完全生成式方法更透明、更可靠且具有更清晰审计途径的方案。

</details>


### [12] [When Less Is More: Simplicity Beats Complexity for Physics-Constrained InSAR Phase Unwrapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00896)
*Prabhjot Singh,Manmeet Singh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文通过大规模消融实验证明，在InSAR相位解缠这一物理约束地球物理回归任务中，简单的Vanilla U-Net（7.76M参数）在性能（R²=0.834, RMSE=1.01cm）和推理速度（2.92ms）上均优于复杂的注意力机制模型，揭示了“复杂度惩罚”现象，并指出注意力机制会引入非物理的高频伪影。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 挑战当前InSAR相位解缠领域盲目采用高复杂度计算机视觉架构（如注意力机制）的趋势，验证这些架构是否真正适用于物理约束的地球物理回归任务，并弥合“发表到实践”的鸿沟。

Method: 在LiCSAR全球基准数据集（20帧、39,724个图块、6.51亿像素）上，进行了首个大规模架构消融研究，对比Vanilla U-Net与基于注意力机制的模型，并利用功率谱密度（PSD）分析从物理角度解释性能差异。

Result: Vanilla U-Net（7.76M参数）以R²=0.834和RMSE=1.01cm超越11.37M参数的注意力模型，R²提升34%，RMSE降低51%；推理延迟2.92ms（2.5倍加速），满足子100ms预警需求；PSD分析表明注意力机制会引入>0.3 cycles/pixel的非物理高频伪影，违反弹性形变的平滑性约束。

Conclusion: 对于平滑场回归任务，卷积局部性优于现代复杂架构，倡导在地球物理遥感中采用物理信息引导的简单模型。

Original Abstract: Operational phase unwrapping is the primary computational bottleneck in InSAR-based volcanic and seismic monitoring. We challenge the industry trend of adopting high-complexity computer vision architectures, such as attention mechanisms, without validating their suitability for physics-constrained geophysical regression. We present the first large-scale architectural ablation study on a global LiCSAR benchmark (20 frames, 39,724 patches, 651M pixels). Our results reveal a significant "complexity penalty": a vanilla U-Net (7.76M parameters) achieves $R^2=0.834$ and RMSE $= 1.01$ cm, outperforming 11.37M-parameter attention-based models by 34% in $R^2$ and 51% in RMSE. Power Spectral Density (PSD) analysis provides the physical justification: while attention excels at capturing sharp semantic edges in natural images, it injects unphysical high-frequency artifacts ($>0.3$ cycles/pixel) into geophysical fields, violating the fundamental smoothness constraints of elastic surface deformation. With a 2.92ms inference latency (a $2.5\times$ speedup), the vanilla U-Net is the only candidate to comfortably meet the sub-100ms requirement for operational early-warning systems. This work bridges the "publication-to-practice" gap by proving that convolutional locality outperforms modern complexity for smooth-field regression, advocating for physics-informed simplicity in ML4RS. Code available at https://github.com/prabhjotschugh/When-Less-is-More-InSAR-Phase-Unwrapping

中文摘要翻译: 运算相位解缠是基于InSAR的火山与地震监测中的主要计算瓶颈。我们挑战了业界采用高复杂度计算机视觉架构（如注意力机制）而未经其是否适用于物理约束地球物理回归验证的趋势。我们在全球LiCSAR基准（20帧、39,724个图块、6.51亿像素）上进行了首个大规模架构消融研究。结果揭示了显著的"复杂度惩罚"：一个Vanilla U-Net（7.76M参数）达到R²=0.834和RMSE=1.01 cm，在R²上超越11.37M参数的注意力模型34%，在RMSE上超越51%。功率谱密度（PSD）分析提供了物理解释：注意力机制虽擅长捕捉自然图像中尖锐的语义边缘，但会向地球物理场注入非物理的高频伪影（>0.3 cycles/pixel），违反了弹性地表形变的基本平滑性约束。凭借2.92ms的推理延迟（2.5倍加速），Vanilla U-Net是唯一能轻松满足运行早期预警系统子100ms要求的候选方案。这项工作通过证明卷积局部性在平滑场回归中优于现代复杂度，弥合了"发表到实践"的差距，倡导在地球物理遥感中采用物理信息引导的简约性。代码见https://github.com/prabhjotschugh/When-Less-is-More-InSAR-Phase-Unwrapping

### [13] [LatentDiff: Scaling Semantic Dataset Comparison to Millions of Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00899)
*James Flora,Kowshik Thopalli,Akshay R. Kulkarni,Weng-Keen Wong,Shusen Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LatentDiff提出了一种在预训练视觉编码器的潜空间中进行可扩展语义数据集比较的框架，通过稀疏自编码器散度测试和密度比估计实现高效且可解释的语义差异识别，并在新基准Noisy-Diff上展现出优越的鲁棒性和准确性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于标题的语义数据集比较方法计算成本高昂，且在面对真实世界中稀疏分布偏移（仅少量图像存在语义差异）时表现不佳，亟需一种高效、可扩展且鲁棒的替代方案。

Method: 在预训练视觉编码器的潜空间内，结合稀疏自编码器（Sparse Autoencoder）的散度测试与密度比估计，实现可解释的语义差异识别。

Result: LatentDiff在准确性上优于现有方法，且对极端稀疏的语义差异（图像比例从5%到低于1%）表现出鲁棒性；同时构建了Noisy-Diff基准以模拟此类真实分布偏移。

Conclusion: LatentDiff为语义数据集比较提供了一种计算高效、可解释且鲁棒的解决方案，特别适用于仅有极小比例图像存在语义差异的实际场景。

Original Abstract: We present LatentDiff, a scalable framework for semantic dataset comparison that operates directly in the latent space of pretrained vision encoders. By combining sparse autoencoder-based divergence testing with density ratio estimation, LatentDiff identifies interpretable semantic differences between datasets at a fraction of the computational cost of caption-based alternatives. We also introduce Noisy-Diff, a benchmark capturing realistic sparse distribution shifts that cause existing methods to struggle. Experiments demonstrate that LatentDiff achieves superior accuracy while remaining robust to settings where an extremely small fraction of images (from 5% to <1% ) differ semantically.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了LatentDiff，一种可扩展的语义数据集比较框架，它直接在预训练视觉编码器的潜空间中操作。通过将基于稀疏自编码器的散度测试与密度比估计相结合，LatentDiff能够以远低于基于标题的替代方法的计算成本，识别数据集之间可解释的语义差异。我们还引入了Noisy-Diff，一个基准测试，用于捕捉导致现有方法失效的真实稀疏分布偏移。实验表明，LatentDiff在实现优越准确性的同时，对仅有极小比例图像（从5%到低于1%）存在语义差异的设置保持鲁棒性。

### [14] [Validation of Whole-Slide Foundation Models for Image Retrieval in TCGA Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00902)
*Tianhao Lei,Parsa Esmaeilkhani,Saghir Alfasly,Wataru Uegami,Judy C. Boughey,Matthew P. Goetz,Krishna R. Kalari,H. R. Tizhoosh*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了基础模型在计算病理学全切片图像检索中的表现，发现性能差异主要源于器官和诊断类型而非架构，现有方法存在明显天花板，远未达到临床部署标准。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 尽管基础模型在计算病理学中广泛应用，但其在全切片图像检索任务中相对于传统的基于patch和监督聚合方法的实际增益尚不明确，本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 在TCGA数据集上（9,387张诊断切片，覆盖17个器官和60种诊断），采用留一患者法进行基准测试，比较了四种预训练的切片基础模型、基于注意力机制的多实例学习（ABMIL）聚合器以及五种采样密度下的patch级检索方法。

Result: TITAN模型整体最优但优势微弱；ABMIL和patch方法在Top-1和Top-3精度上相当；性能在器官和诊断间差异大于架构间差异；形态学独特实体接近上限，而罕见、异质和近缘亚型仍具挑战；最佳模型在TCGA上仅达约68%±21%的检索精度，部分亚型在所有方法中准确率为0%。

Conclusion: 不存在普遍最优的架构，应支持按器官基准测试、诊断感知或集成策略、更强特征表示及多模态检索框架；当前形态学表示存在根本局限，临床部署前仍需实质性进展。

Original Abstract: Foundation models are reshaping computational histopathology, yet their value for whole-slide image retrieval relative to strong patch-based and supervised aggregation baselines remains unclear. We benchmarked ten pipelines on 9,387 diagnostic slides spanning 17 organs and 60 diagnoses from The Cancer Genome Atlas (TCGA) using patient-level leave-one-patient-out evaluation. Methods included four pre-trained slide foundation models, a supervised attention-based multiple instance learning (ABMIL) aggregator on patch embeddings, and patch-level retrieval across five sampling densities.
  Performance varied more across organs and diagnoses than across architectures. Although the slide foundation model TITAN achieved the strongest overall results, its advantage was modest; ABMIL and patch-based methods reached comparable Top-1 and Top-3 accuracy, with no model consistently dominant. Morphologically distinctive entities approached ceiling performance, while rare, heterogeneous, and closely related subtypes remained challenging. Misclassifications aligned with organs exhibiting known inter-observer variability, suggesting an intrinsic ceiling for morphology-only retrieval.
  Performance was driven primarily by patch-level feature representations, with limited benefit from slide-level aggregation, indicating aggregation may be unnecessary in many settings. These findings argue against a universally optimal architecture and instead support organ-resolved benchmarking, diagnosis-aware or ensemble strategies, stronger feature representations, and multimodal retrieval frameworks. Notably, even the best model achieved only $\approx 68\% \pm 21\%$ retrieval accuracy on TCGA, and some subtypes showed $0\%$ accuracy across all methods, highlighting fundamental limitations of morphology-based representations and the need for substantial progress before reliable clinical deployment.

中文摘要翻译: 基础模型正在重塑计算病理学，但它们在全切片图像检索中相对于强大的基于patch和监督聚合基线的价值仍不明确。我们在来自癌症基因组图谱（TCGA）的9,387张诊断切片（涵盖17个器官和60种诊断）上，采用患者级留一患者法评估了十种流水线。方法包括四种预训练的切片基础模型、一种在patch嵌入上训练的基于注意力的多实例学习（ABMIL）聚合器以及五种采样密度下的patch级检索。性能在不同器官和诊断之间的差异大于不同架构之间的差异。尽管切片基础模型TITAN取得了最强的整体结果，但其优势微弱；ABMIL和基于patch的方法达到了可比的Top-1和Top-3精度，且没有模型始终占优。形态学上独特的实体接近性能上限，而罕见、异质及密切相关的亚型仍然具有挑战性。错误分类与已知存在观察者间变异性的器官一致，表明纯形态学检索存在内在上限。性能主要受patch级特征表示驱动，切片级聚合带来的收益有限，表明在许多场景中聚合可能并非必要。这些发现反对存在普遍最优的架构，转而支持按器官基准测试、诊断感知或集成策略、更强特征表示以及多模态检索框架。值得注意的是，即使是最佳模型在TCGA上也仅达到约68%±21%的检索精度，且某些亚型在所有方法上的准确率均为0%，凸显了基于形态学表示的根本局限性，以及在实际临床部署前仍需取得实质性进展。

### [15] [TRIP-Evaluate: An Open Multimodal Benchmark for Evaluating Large Models in Transportation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00907)
*Han Gong,Zhen Zhou,Yunyang Shi,Yan Tan,Jinbiao Huo,Qi Hong,Zhiyuan Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TRIP-Evaluate 是一个面向交通领域大模型和多模态大模型的多模态基准测试，包含837个文本、图像和点云项目，通过角色-任务-知识分类体系支持细粒度诊断，实验表明模型在文本任务上表现提升，但在多步工程计算、规则约束推理、多模态场景理解和点云理解方面仍存在明显不足。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有通用基准无法验证模型是否能在交通领域正确应用法规、执行可验证的工程计算或可靠地解读交通场景，而少数公开的交通基准范围狭窄且不支持跨文本、图像和点云数据的细粒度诊断。

Method: 构建了一个包含837个项目的开放多模态基准，采用角色-任务-知识分类体系覆盖车辆、交通管理、出行者和规划设计功能，标注了能力、模态和难度标签，标准化了项目构建、质量控制、提示、解码和评分流程以提升跨模型可比性。

Result: 当前版本包含596个文本项目、198个图像项目和43个点云项目。多模型评估显示，文本任务性能正在提升，但在多步工程计算、规则约束推理、多模态场景理解和点云理解方面仍存在显著弱点。

Conclusion: TRIP-Evaluate 为交通领域的模型选择、回归测试和安全部署提供了一个可复现、可诊断且符合工程实践的评估基线。

Original Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) and multimodal large models (MLLMs) are increasingly used for transportation tasks such as regulation question answering, traffic management support, engineering review, and autonomous-driving scene reasoning. Yet transportation workflows are rule-intensive, computation-intensive, safety-critical, and inherently multimodal. Existing general benchmarks provide limited evidence of whether a model can apply regulations correctly, perform verifiable engineering calculations, or interpret traffic scenes reliably, while the small number of public transportation benchmarks remain narrow in scope and rarely support fine-grained diagnosis across text, images, and point-cloud data. To address this gap, we present TRIP-Evaluate, an open multimodal benchmark for large models in transportation. The benchmark organizes 837 items using a role-task-knowledge taxonomy that covers vehicle, traffic-management, traveler, and planning-and-design functions. Each item is annotated with capability, modality, and difficulty labels, enabling diagnosis from overall accuracy down to specific failure modes. The current release includes 596 text items, 198 image items, and 43 point-cloud items. TRIP-Evaluate also standardizes item construction, quality control, prompting, decoding, and scoring to improve cross-model comparability. Results on a diverse panel of models show that text-based performance is improving, but substantial weaknesses remain in multi-step engineering calculation, rule-constrained reasoning, multimodal scene understanding, and point-cloud understanding. Overall, TRIP-Evaluate provides a reproducible, diagnosable, and engineering-aligned evaluation baseline for model selection, regression testing, and safer deployment in transportation applications.

中文摘要翻译: 大语言模型和多模态大模型越来越多地被用于交通任务，如法规问答、交通管理支持、工程审查和自动驾驶场景推理。然而，交通工作流具有规则密集型、计算密集型、安全关键性和固有模态多样性等特点。现有通用基准很难验证模型是否能正确应用法规、执行可验证的工程计算或可靠地解读交通场景，而少数公开的交通基准范围狭窄，很少支持跨文本、图像和点云数据的细粒度诊断。为填补这一空白，我们提出了TRIP-Evaluate，一个面向交通领域大模型的开放多模态基准。该基准采用角色-任务-知识分类体系，涵盖车辆、交通管理、出行者及规划设计功能，共组织837个项目。每个项目标注了能力、模态和难度标签，支持从整体准确率到特定故障模式的诊断。当前版本包含596个文本项目、198个图像项目和43个点云项目。TRIP-Evaluate还标准化了项目构建、质量控制、提示、解码和评分流程，以提升跨模型可比性。对多种模型的评估结果表明，模型在文本任务上的性能正在提升，但在多步工程计算、规则约束推理、多模态场景理解和点云理解方面仍存在明显不足。总体而言，TRIP-Evaluate为交通应用中的模型选择、回归测试和更安全的部署提供了可复现、可诊断且符合工程实践的评估基线。

</details>


### [16] [When Good OCR Is Not Enough: Benchmarking OCR Robustness for Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00911)
*Lin Sun,Wang Dexian,Jingang Huang,Linglin Zhang,Change Jia,Zhengwei Cheng,Xiangzheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一个面向工业RAG系统的OCR基准测试InduOCRBench，涵盖11种复杂文档类型。实验发现，在真实工业场景下，现有SOTA OCR模型性能显著下降，且高OCR精度（低WER/CER）并不必然带来好的下游RAG效果——结构和语义错误即使不影响字符级指标，也会导致严重的检索失败。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的OCR基准测试主要依赖字符级指标（如WER/CER），无法充分衡量在真实工业RAG系统下游任务中的实际效果，因此需要设计一个更贴近工业场景的OCR基准。

Method: 构建了涵盖11种挑战性文档类型的基准集（包括极端版式、高分辨率页面、复杂/水印背景、非标准阅读顺序的历史文档、装饰性文字、表格和数学公式等），并在可控的"OCR优先RAG流水线"下评估近期SOTA OCR模型。

Result: 1) SOTA OCR模型在工业文档上性能显著下降；2) 高OCR精度不必然带来好的RAG性能，结构和语义错误即使WER/CER很低也会导致检索失败；3) 这种不匹配与文档类别相关，同时存在于检索侧和生成侧，且在多种OCR优先流水线选择下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 现有OCR评估指标（字符级）不足以反映工业RAG系统的真实需求，需要关注结构和语义层面的错误对下游任务的影响。

Original Abstract: Industrial Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems depend on optical character recognition (OCR) to transform visual documents into text. Existing OCR benchmarks rely on character-level metrics, which inadequately measure downstream RAG effectiveness under real-world conditions. We introduce an OCR benchmark for industrial RAG systems covering 11 challenging document types, including extreme layouts, high-resolution pages, complex or watermarked backgrounds, historical documents with non-standard reading orders, visually decorated text, and documents containing tables and mathematical formulas. Evaluating recent SOTA OCR models under a controlled OCR-first RAG pipeline shows clear performance degradation on realistic industrial documents despite strong conventional benchmark scores. We find that high OCR accuracy does not necessarily translate into strong downstream RAG performance: structural and semantic errors can cause substantial retrieval failures even when WER/CER remains low. Further analysis shows that this mismatch is category-dependent, arises through both retrieval-side and downstream generation-side failures, and remains stable across representative OCR-first pipeline choices. The benchmark is publicly available at https://github.com/Qihoo360/InduOCRBench.

中文摘要翻译: 工业检索增强生成（RAG）系统依赖光学字符识别（OCR）将视觉文档转换为文本。现有的OCR基准测试依赖字符级指标，无法充分衡量在真实工业条件下下游RAG系统的有效性。我们提出了一个面向工业RAG系统的OCR基准测试，涵盖11种具有挑战性的文档类型，包括极端版式、高分辨率页面、复杂或水印背景、非标准阅读顺序的历史文档、视觉装饰文本，以及包含表格和数学公式的文档。在受控的OCR优先RAG流水线下评估近期SOTA OCR模型的结果表明，尽管这些模型在传统基准测试中表现优异，但在真实工业文档上性能显著下降。我们发现，高OCR精度并不必然转化为优异的下游RAG性能：即使词错误率（WER）和字符错误率（CER）较低，结构和语义错误也可能导致严重的检索失败。进一步分析表明，这种不匹配与文档类别相关，同时出现在检索侧和下游生成侧的失败中，并且在多种代表性OCR优先流水线选择下保持稳定。该基准测试已在https://github.com/Qihoo360/InduOCRBench公开。

### [17] [Object-Level Explanations for Image Geolocation Models: a GeoGuessr use-case](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00912)
*Emilie Durrieu,Christophe Hurter,Philippe Muller,Victor Boutin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种以对象为中心的分析流程，通过将归因图分解为可解释的感知元素，来探究地理定位模型所使用的视觉证据。实验表明，归因引导的裁剪区域比随机裁剪能保留更多预测信息。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有归因方法（如Grad-CAM）通常高亮扩散区域而非连贯的视觉实体，难以将模型预测与具体物体或可感知的模式联系起来，因此需要一种能够在物体层面分析地理定位模型依赖证据的方法。

Method: 从归因图中提取显著区域并将其分割为类物体元素，通过删除和插入测试评估其预测相关性，并将归因引导的裁剪与具有相似覆盖范围的随机裁剪进行对比。

Result: 在三国家基准数据集上的实验表明，归因引导的裁剪始终比随机裁剪保留了更多用于模型预测的信息。

Conclusion: 归因图可以被分解为可解释、可感知的元素，为地理定位模型的物体级分析提供了一种可行途径。

Original Abstract: When humans play geolocation games such as GeoGuessr, they rely on concrete visual cues, such as road markings, vegetation, or architectural details, to infer where an image was captured. Whether image geolocation models rely on similar object-level evidence remains difficult to determine, as attribution methods like Grad-CAM typically highlight diffuse regions rather than coherent visual entities, making it difficult to link model predictions to specific objects or perceptible patterns. In this work, we propose an object-centric analysis pipeline to investigate the visual evidence used by geolocation models. Starting from attribution maps, we extract salient regions and segment them into object-like elements. We evaluate their predictive relevance through deletion and insertion tests, comparing attributionguided crops to randomly selected regions with similar coverage. Experiments on a three-country benchmark show that attribution-guided crops consistently retain more information for the model's prediction than random crops. These results suggest that attribution maps can be decomposed into interpretable, perceptible elements, providing a step toward object-level analysis of geolocation models.

中文摘要翻译: 当人类玩GeoGuessr这类地理定位游戏时，他们会依赖具体的视觉线索，如道路标线、植被或建筑细节，来推断图像拍摄地点。图像地理定位模型是否依赖类似的物体级证据仍然难以确定，因为Grad-CAM等归因方法通常高亮扩散的区域而非连贯的视觉实体，这使得难以将模型预测与特定物体或可感知的模式联系起来。本文提出一种以对象为中心的分析流程，用于探究地理定位模型所使用的视觉证据。我们从归因图出发，提取显著区域并将其分割为类物体元素。通过删除和插入测试评估这些元素的预测相关性，将归因引导的裁剪与具有相似覆盖范围的随机裁剪进行对比。在三国家基准数据集上的实验表明，归因引导的裁剪始终比随机裁剪保留了更多用于模型预测的信息。这些结果表明，归因图可以被分解为可解释、可感知的元素，为地理定位模型的物体级分析提供了可行的一步。

### [18] [SAMamba3D: adapting Segment Anything for generalizable 3D segmentation of multiphase pore-scale images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.00916)
*Rui Zhang,Xianzhi Song,Linqi Zhu,Branko Bijeljic,Gensheng Li,Martin J. Blunt*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SAMamba3D提出了一种参数高效框架，通过将冻结的SAM编码器与Mamba体素上下文建模及跨尺度特征交互结合，实现了对多相孔隙尺度X射线岩石图像的可泛化三维分割，无需针对不同岩石类型、流体模式或扫描条件重新训练。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前多相孔隙尺度岩石图像的三维分割方法通常依赖特定数据集，每当岩石类型、流体模式、扫描仪或采集条件变化时都需要重新训练或大量微调。虽然基础模型（如SAM）提供了强大的二维边界先验，但无法直接应用于三维数据。因此，需要一种能够泛化到不同条件下且无需大量重新训练的三维分割方法。

Method: SAMamba3D采用参数高效框架，冻结大部分SAM编码器以保留二维边界先验，同时将其与基于Mamba的体积上下文建模以及渐进式跨尺度特征交互模块相结合，实现对三维孔隙尺度图像的分割。

Result: 在砂岩和碳酸盐岩数据集上，涵盖不同流体、润湿性和扫描条件，SAMamba3D匹配或超越了当前三维基线方法的性能，同时减少了对特定案例重新训练的需求。分割图像保留了具有物理意义的描述符，包括流体饱和度、连通性和界面形态。

Conclusion: SAMamba3D能够在多种岩石类型、流体模式和扫描条件下实现可靠的三维孔隙尺度分割，显著降低了数据集特定重新训练的需求，为大规模三维多相图像的快速分析提供了更可靠的方案。

Original Abstract: Reliable segmentation of multiphase pore-scale X-ray images of rocks is necessary to quantify fluid saturation, connectivity, and interfacial geometry. However, current 3D segmentation methods are typically dataset-specific, requiring retraining or extensive fine-tuning whenever rock type, fluid pattern, scanner, or acquisition conditions change. Foundation models such as the Segment Anything Model (SAM) provide strong 2D boundary priors, but they are not directly applicable to 3D data.
  We present SAMamba3D, a parameter-efficient framework that adapts a largely frozen SAM encoder to generalizable 3D pore-scale segmentation by coupling it with Mamba-based volumetric context modeling and progressive cross-scale feature interaction. For sandstone and carbonate datasets, with different fluids, wettability, and scanning conditions, SAMamba3D matches or outperforms current 3D baselines while reducing the need for case-specific retraining. The resulting segmented images preserve physically meaningful descriptors, including fluid saturation, connectivity, and interface morphology, enabling more reliable and rapid analysis of large 3D multiphase images.

中文摘要翻译: 对多相孔隙尺度X射线岩石图像进行可靠分割是量化流体饱和度、连通性和界面几何结构的必要条件。然而，当前的三维分割方法通常依赖于特定数据集，每当岩石类型、流体模式、扫描仪或采集条件发生变化时，都需要重新训练或进行大量微调。诸如Segment Anything Model（SAM）等基础模型提供了强大的二维边界先验，但它们无法直接应用于三维数据。本文提出SAMamba3D，一种参数高效框架，通过将大部分冻结的SAM编码器与基于Mamba的体积上下文建模及渐进式跨尺度特征交互相结合，使其适配于可泛化的三维孔隙尺度分割。在砂岩和碳酸盐岩数据集上，针对不同流体、润湿性和扫描条件，SAMamba3D匹配或超越了当前三维基线方法的性能，同时减少了对特定案例重新训练的需求。最终的分割图像保留了具有物理意义的描述符，包括流体饱和度、连通性和界面形态，从而能够对大规模三维多相图像进行更可靠、更快速的分析。

### [19] [WildTableBench: Benchmarking Multimodal Foundation Models on Table Understanding In the Wild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01018)
*Junzhe Huang,Xiaoxiao Sun,Yan Yang,Yuxuan Hou,Ruotian Zhang,Sirui Li,Hehe Fan,Serena Yeung-Levy,Xin Yu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出WildTableBench，首个面向真实世界表格图像的多模态问答基准，发现现有最强模型准确率仅略超50%，普遍存在结构感知和推理缺陷。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有表格理解评测多基于结构化文本或干净渲染图像，忽略了真实场景表格图像的视觉复杂性（如多样化布局和领域），缺乏对该场景下多模态基础模型能力的系统评估。

Method: 构建WildTableBench基准，包含402张来自在线论坛和网站的真实表格图像及928个手工标注的多类型问答对，覆盖5大类17个子类，并对21个前沿多模态基础模型进行评估和诊断分析。

Result: 仅一个模型准确率超过50%（其余在4.1%-49.9%之间），诊断分析揭示模型在结构感知和推理方面存在持续性弱点。

Conclusion: WildTableBench可作为有价值的诊断基准，揭示了当前多模态基础模型在真实表格图像理解上的显著不足，为后续改进提供了方向。

Original Abstract: Using multimodal foundation models to analyze table images is a high-value yet challenging application in consumer and enterprise scenarios. Despite its importance, current evaluations rely largely on structured-text tables or clean rendered images, leaving the visual complexity of in-the-wild table images underexplored. Such images feature varied layouts and diverse domains that demand sophisticated structural perception and numerical reasoning. To bridge this gap, we introduce WildTableBench, the first question-answering benchmark for naturally occurring table images from real-world settings. WildTableBench comprises 402 high-information-density table images collected from online forums and websites across diverse domains, together with 928 manually annotated and verified questions spanning 17 subtypes across five categories. We evaluate 21 frontier proprietary and open-source multimodal foundation models on this benchmark. Only one model exceeds 50% accuracy, while all remaining models range from 4.1% to 49.9%. We further conduct diagnostic analyses to characterize model failures and reveal persistent weaknesses in structural perception and reasoning. These results and analyses provide useful insights into current model capabilities and establish WildTableBench as a valuable diagnostic benchmark for table image understanding.

中文摘要翻译: 利用多模态基础模型分析表格图像是一个在消费和企业场景中高价值但具有挑战性的应用。尽管其重要性，当前的评估主要依赖结构化文本表格或干净的渲染图像，忽略了真实世界表格图像的视觉复杂性。此类图像具有多样化的布局和领域，需要复杂的结构感知和数值推理。为填补这一空白，我们提出了WildTableBench，首个面向真实场景中自然出现的表格图像的问答基准。WildTableBench包含402张来自在线论坛和网站的高信息密度表格图像，覆盖多个领域，以及928个手工标注和验证的问题，涵盖5大类17个子类。我们在该基准上评估了21个前沿专有和开源多模态基础模型，仅一个模型准确率超过50%，其余模型准确率在4.1%至49.9%之间。我们进一步进行了诊断分析以刻画模型失败模式，揭示了结构感知和推理方面的持续性弱点。这些结果和分析为当前模型能力提供了有价值的见解，并将WildTableBench确立为表格图像理解领域有价值的诊断基准。

### [21] [WILD SAM: A Simulated-and-Real Data Augmentation for Autonomous Driving Perception under Challenging Weather](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01081)
*Hamed Khatounabadi,Xiaohu Lu,Hayder Radha*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出WILD和WILD SAM两种方法，分别通过伪标签去噪和混合训练策略，解决恶劣天气下目标检测器的域偏移问题，在四季数据集上AP提升高达13%。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有最先进目标检测器在恶劣天气下性能显著下降，造成自动驾驶的域偏移问题。现有方法依赖合成数据或伪标签，但伪标签在恶劣天气下噪声大，未被充分利用。

Method: 提出WILD框架用于过滤恶劣天气下生成的噪声伪标签；进一步提出WILD SAM混合训练方法，结合伪标签去噪和基于仿真的训练方案，同时利用目标恶劣天气域的真实数据。

Result: 在四季数据集（雨雪场景）上验证，AP提升高达13%，显著缩小了天气导致的性能差距。

Conclusion: WILD和WILD SAM有效缓解了天气引起的域偏移问题，为恶劣天气下的目标检测提供了可行方案，代码已开源。

Original Abstract: The performance of state-of-the-art object detectors degrades significantly under adverse weather, causing a safety-critical domain shift problem for autonomous vehicles. Recent efforts address this problem by relying on synthetic data to train the object detectors, which limits their real-world applicability. Meanwhile, pseudo-labeling is widely used for cross-dataset domain adaptation problems. However, these methods have not been exploited by weather-based domain adaptation approaches due to the noisy nature of such labels generated under harsh weather conditions. In this paper, we propose two new approaches to mitigate this weather-induced domain shift. First, we propose a Weather-Induced pseudo Label Denoising (WILD) framework that filters noisy pseudo labels generated by real data captured under adverse weather conditions. Second, we develop a novel hybrid training methodology, WILD SAM, that exploits both pseudo-label denoising and simulation-based training solutions while using real-data from the target harsh-weather domain. We validate both proposed approaches, WILD and WILD SAM, on the recently released Four Seasons dataset across rainy and snowy scenarios. Experiments show that the proposed frameworks improve Average Precision (AP) up to 13\% and significantly reduce the weather-induced performance gap relative to the baseline. The code is available at: https://github.com/Kh-Hamed/WILD-SAM

中文摘要翻译: 最先进的目标检测器在恶劣天气下的性能会显著下降，这对自动驾驶汽车造成了安全关键性的域偏移问题。近期的工作依赖合成数据来训练目标检测器，这限制了其在真实世界中的适用性。同时，伪标签被广泛用于跨数据集的域自适应问题。然而，由于在恶劣天气条件下生成的伪标签存在噪声特性，这些方法尚未被基于天气的域自适应方法所利用。本文提出了两种新方法来缓解这种天气引起的域偏移。首先，我们提出了一个天气诱导的伪标签去噪（WILD）框架，用于过滤在恶劣天气条件下捕获的真实数据所产生的噪声伪标签。其次，我们开发了一种新的混合训练方法WILD SAM，该方法同时利用了伪标签去噪和基于仿真的训练方案，同时使用来自目标恶劣天气域的真实数据。我们在最近发布的四季数据集的雨雪场景下验证了所提出的WILD和WILD SAM方法。实验表明，所提出的框架将平均精度（AP）提升了高达13%，并显著缩小了与基线相比的天气诱导性能差距。代码已在https://github.com/Kh-Hamed/WILD-SAM开源。

</details>


### [22] [Disciplined Diffusion: Text-to-Image Diffusion Model against NSFW Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01113)
*Chi Zhang,Changjia Zhu,Xiaowen Li,Yao Liu,Zhuo Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Disciplined Diffusion (DDiffusion)，一种通过语义检索和局部编辑来抵御NSFW内容生成的鲁棒文本到图像扩散模型，克服了传统二值过滤器的脆弱性和高误报率问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有安全过滤器依赖文本分类器或图像检查器进行二值阻断（允许/阻止），存在两个主要缺陷：(1) 易受对抗性攻击（通过修改关键词绕过检测）；(2) 高误报率损害良性用户体验。需要一种更鲁棒且细粒度的安全机制。

Method: (1) 语义检索机制：通过评估提示与概念分布的匹配度来检测隐含恶意语义，而非脆弱的成对相似性；(2) 局部编辑方法：在扩散过程中定位并选择性编辑生成图像中的有害区域，而非整体阻断。

Result: DDiffusion能有效抑制恶意内容生成，同时保持良性提示的生成保真度，避免了现有探测攻击所依赖的二值允许/拒绝信号。

Conclusion: 通过返回局部净化的图像而非统一阻断，DDiffusion在安全性和可用性之间取得了更好的平衡，为文本到图像模型的安全部署提供了更鲁棒的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) diffusion models have the ability to build high-quality pictures from text prompts, but they pose safety concerns because they can generate offensive or disturbing imagery when provided with harmful inputs. Existing safety filters typically rely on text-based classifiers or image-based checkers that completely block the output upon detecting a threat, issuing an explicit allow/block feedback signal to the user. This binary strategy leaves models vulnerable to adversarial attacks that alter keywords to bypass detection, and it causes high false-alarm rates that degrade the experience for benign users. To address such vulnerabilities, we propose Disciplined Diffusion (DDiffusion), a novel robust text-to-image diffusion that counters Not Safe For Work (NSFW) generation by uncovering implicit malicious semantics in prompt embeddings. DDiffusion leverages a semantic retrieval mechanism to evaluate prompts against concept distributions rather than relying on brittle pairwise similarity. Furthermore, it employs a localization method during the diffusion process to selectively edit only the harmful regions of the generated image. By returning locally sanitized images instead of applying uniform blocking, DDiffusion suppresses malicious content while preserving generation fidelity for benign prompts and avoiding the binary allow-deny signal on which existing probing attacks rely.

中文摘要翻译: 文本到图像（T2I）扩散模型能够根据文本提示生成高质量图片，但由于可能根据有害输入生成冒犯性或令人不安的图像，引发了安全隐患。现有的安全过滤器通常依赖基于文本的分类器或基于图像的检查器，在检测到威胁时完全阻断输出，向用户发出明确的允许/阻断反馈信号。这种二值策略使模型容易受到对抗性攻击——攻击者通过修改关键词来绕过检测，同时导致高误报率，损害了良性用户的体验。针对这些脆弱性，我们提出了Disciplined Diffusion（DDiffusion），一种新颖的鲁棒文本到图像扩散方法，通过揭示提示嵌入中的隐含恶意语义来对抗Not Safe For Work（NSFW）内容的生成。DDiffusion利用语义检索机制评估提示与概念分布的匹配程度，而非依赖脆弱的成对相似性。此外，它在扩散过程中采用定位方法，选择性编辑生成图像中仅有的有害区域。通过返回局部净化的图像而非应用统一阻断，DDiffusion抑制了恶意内容，同时保持了良性提示的生成保真度，并避免了现有探测攻击所依赖的二值允许/拒绝信号。

### [23] [ScribbleEdit: Synthetic Data for Image Editing with Scribbles and Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01135)
*Anya Ji,George Ma,Téa Wright,Yiming Zhang,David Chan,Alane Suhr,Somayeh Sojoudi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ScribbleEdit，一个大规模合成数据集，通过结合自然语言指令和手绘涂鸦来实现精确可控的图像编辑，实验表明在该数据集上微调能显著提升模型的空间对齐和语义一致性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 用户难以同时通过单一模态精确表达图像编辑所需的空间布局和语义细节：文本描述缺乏空间精确性，手绘涂鸦无法表达颜色、纹理等细节属性。现有模型因缺乏专门训练数据而难以联合解释抽象涂鸦和文本指令。

Method: 通过一个合成pipeline自动生成源-目标图像对（基于inpainting），然后与人工绘制的涂鸦和VLM生成的文本指令配对，构建ScribbleEdit大规模合成数据集，并基于该数据集微调扩散模型和自回归统一多模态图像编辑模型。

Result: 现成的模型难以处理抽象涂鸦输入；在ScribbleEdit合成数据集上微调后，模型生成空间对齐且语义一致编辑结果的能力得到显著提升。

Conclusion: ScribbleEdit数据集有效弥合了文本和涂鸦两种模态之间的鸿沟，为多模态可控图像编辑提供了关键训练数据，提升了模型在联合理解抽象涂鸦与文本指令方面的能力。

Original Abstract: Recent progress in generative models has significantly advanced image editing capabilities, yet precise and intuitive user control remains difficult. Specifically, users often struggle to communicate both exact spatial layouts and specific semantic details simultaneously. While natural language instructions effectively convey high-level semantics like texture and color, they lack spatial specificity. Conversely, freehand scribbles provide rough spatial boundaries but cannot express detailed visual attributes. Consequently, achieving precise control requires combining both modalities. However, existing models struggle to jointly interpret abstract scribbles alongside text due to a lack of specialized training data.
  In this work, we introduce ScribbleEdit, a large-scale synthetic dataset designed to bridge this gap by combining natural language instructions with freehand scribble inputs for more accurate, controllable edits. We construct this dataset through a synthetic pipeline that automatically generates source-target image pairs via inpainting, which are then paired with human-drawn scribbles and VLM-generated text instructions. Using ScribbleEdit, we evaluate and finetune both diffusion-based and autoregressive unified multimodal image editing models. Our experiments reveal that while off-the-shelf models struggle with abstract scribble inputs, finetuning on our synthetic dataset significantly improves their ability to generate spatially aligned and semantically consistent edits.

中文摘要翻译: 近年来生成模型的进展显著推动了图像编辑能力的发展，但精确且直观的用户控制仍然困难。具体而言，用户常常难以同时传达精确的空间布局和特定的语义细节。自然语言指令虽然能有效传达纹理和颜色等高层语义，但缺乏空间精确性。相反，手绘涂鸦能提供粗略的空间边界，却无法表达详细的视觉属性。因此，实现精确控制需要结合两种模态。然而，现有模型因缺乏专门的训练数据，难以联合解释抽象的涂鸦与文本。在本工作中，我们引入了ScribbleEdit——一个大规模合成数据集，旨在通过结合自然语言指令与手绘涂鸦输入来实现更准确、可控的编辑。我们通过一个合成pipeline自动生成基于inpainting的源-目标图像对，再与人工绘制的涂鸦和VLM生成的文本指令配对，从而构建该数据集。利用ScribbleEdit，我们评估并微调了基于扩散模型和自回归的统一多模态图像编辑模型。实验结果表明，现成模型难以处理抽象的涂鸦输入，而在我们的合成数据集上进行微调后，模型生成空间对齐且语义一致的编辑结果的能力得到显著提升。

### [24] [Semantic Context-aware mOdality fUsion Transformer (SCOUT): A Context-Aware Multimodal Transformer for Concept-Grounded Pathology Report Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01144)
*Suryakant Singh,Saarthak Kapse,Joel Saltz,Prateek Prasanna*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: SCOUT是一个上下文感知的概念引导多模态框架，通过渐进式视觉特征条件化和自适应多模态融合，在病理报告生成任务上显著优于现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有病理基础模型虽能生成流畅报告，但缺乏临床依据，无法准确表达病理学家观察到的关键诊断概念和关系，根本原因在于难以整合从细胞级到全切片级的异构视觉证据，同时保持可解释性和临床一致性。

Method: 提出SCOUT框架，包含：（1）将局部组织学模式、全切片上下文和专家策划的语义描述符统一到同一学习范式中；（2）通过深度感知的上下文调制渐进式地利用全局切片信息和显式诊断概念对图像表示进行条件化；（3）在文本生成过程中采用自适应多模态融合保持不同表征尺度间的互补性。

Result: 在TCGA-BRCA、MICCAI REG和HistAI三个数据集上，SCOUT在所有数据集上的BLEU-1至BLEU-4和METEOR指标均达到最优，并且在TCGA-BRCA和MICCAI REG上取得最优ROUGE-L。具体地，在TCGA-BRCA上达到0.436/0.303/0.202/0.156的BLEU-1/2/3/4和0.204的METEOR；在REG 2025上达到0.865/0.834/0.805/0.780和0.568。

Conclusion: 渐进式上下文条件化能够有效提升基于临床依据的病理报告生成质量，验证了语义感知的概念引导多模态融合在计算病理学中的有效性。

Original Abstract: Whole-slide images (WSIs) present a fundamental challenge for computational pathology due to their extreme resolution, multi-scale heterogeneity, and the requirement for clinically reliable interpretation. Although recent pathology foundation models have enabled fluent report generation, they often lack clinical grounding, failing to accurately represent key diagnostic concepts and relationships observed by pathologists. This limitation arises from the difficulty of integrating heterogeneous visual evidence spanning fine-grained cellular patterns, slide-level tissue architecture, and high-level diagnostic concepts, while maintaining interpretability and clinical coherence. Here we present SCOUT: Semantic Context-aware mOdality fUsion Transformer, a context-aware concept-grounded multimodal framework for pathology report generation that enables progressive conditioning of image representations by global slide information and explicit diagnostic concepts. The method integrates local histological patterns, whole-slide context, and expert-curated semantic descriptors within a unified learning paradigm, allowing visual features to be dynamically refined throughout the encoding process. By combining depth-aware contextual modulation with adaptive multimodal fusion during text generation, the framework produces clinically coherent reports while preserving complementarity across representational scales. Using CONCH1.5 features, we evaluate SCOUT against WSI-Caption, HistGen, and BiGen on TCGA-BRCA, MICCAI REG, and HistAI. SCOUT achieves the best BLEU-1 to BLEU-4 and METEOR scores on all datasets, plus the best ROUGE-L on TCGA-BRCA and MICCAI REG. On TCGA-BRCA, it reaches 0.436/0.303/0.202/0.156 BLEU-1/2/3/4 and 0.204 METEOR; on REG 2025, it achieves 0.865/0.834/0.805/0.780 and 0.568. These results support progressive contextual conditioning for grounded pathology report generation.

中文摘要翻译: 全切片图像因其极高的分辨率、多尺度异质性以及对临床可靠解释的需求，给计算病理学带来了根本性挑战。尽管最近的病理基础模型已能生成流畅的报告，但它们通常缺乏临床依据，无法准确表达病理学家观察到的关键诊断概念和关系。这一局限性源于难以整合从细粒度细胞模式、切片级组织架构到高层诊断概念的异构视觉证据，同时保持可解释性和临床一致性。本文提出SCOUT：语义上下文感知模态融合Transformer，一种上下文感知的概念引导多模态框架，用于病理报告生成，能够通过全局切片信息和显式诊断概念对图像表示进行渐进式条件化。该方法将局部组织学模式、全切片上下文和专家策划的语义描述符统一在同一个学习范式中，使得视觉特征能够在编码过程中被动态地精炼。通过在文本生成过程中结合深度感知的上下文调制与自适应多模态融合，该框架在保持表征尺度间互补性的同时生成临床连贯的报告。基于CONCH1.5特征，我们在TCGA-BRCA、MICCAI REG和HistAI数据集上对SCOUT与WSI-Caption、HistGen和BiGen进行了评估。SCOUT在所有数据集上均取得了最优的BLEU-1到BLEU-4和METEOR分数，并在TCGA-BRCA和MICCAI REG上取得了最优的ROUGE-L分数。在TCGA-BRCA上，其BLEU-1/2/3/4分别达到0.436/0.303/0.202/0.156，METEOR达到0.204；在REG 2025上，分别为0.865/0.834/0.805/0.780和0.568。这些结果验证了渐进式上下文条件化在基于临床依据的病理报告生成中的有效性。

### [25] [CEZSAR: A Contrastive Embedding Method for Zero-Shot Action Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01165)
*Valter Estevam,Rayson Laroca,Helio Pedrini,David Menotti*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于对比学习的零样本动作识别方法（CEZSAR），通过构建联合嵌入空间并设计自动负采样策略来弥合语义鸿沟和解决域偏移问题，在UCF-101和Kinetics-400数据集上取得了最先进的结果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 零样本动作识别中存在两大挑战：语义鸿沟（文本域与视觉域表示不一致）和域偏移（训练集与测试集分布差异）。现有方法难以同时有效解决这两个问题。

Method: 提出一种基于对比学习的联合嵌入空间模型，将视频与其自然语言描述进行对齐训练；同时设计自动负采样程序来扩充训练数据集，生成视觉外观与无关描述的不配对数据以增强模型判别能力。

Result: 在UCF-101和Kinetics-400数据集上的多种划分配置下均取得了最先进的结果。

Conclusion: 通过对比学习联合嵌入空间并引入自动负采样，有效缓解了语义鸿沟和域偏移问题，提升了零样本动作识别的性能。

Original Abstract: This paper proposes a novel Zero-Shot Action Recognition~(ZSAR) method based on contrastive learning. In ZSAR, we aim to classify examples from classes that were missing during training. Two well-known problems remain in ZSAR: the semantic gap and the domain shift. A semantic gap occurs because label representations come from the textual domain (i.e., language models) and must be associated with visual representations (i.e., CNNs, RNNs, transformer-based). This multimodal nature implies that the semantic properties of the two spaces are not identical. On the other hand, the domain shift arises from differences between the training and test sets and is inherent to ZSAR once the test set is unknown. One of the most promising methods to address both issues is learning joint embedding spaces. Therefore, we propose a new model that encodes videos and sentences in a joint embedding space, trained by aligning videos with their natural-language descriptions. We design an automatic negative sampling procedure to augment the training dataset and generate unpaired data, i.e., visual appearance and unrelated descriptions. Our results are state-of-the-art on the UCF-101 and Kinetics-400 datasets under several split configurations. Our code is available at https://github.com/valterlej/cezsar.

中文摘要翻译: 本文提出了一种基于对比学习的新型零样本动作识别（ZSAR）方法。在ZSAR中，我们的目标是对训练时未出现类别的样本进行分类。ZSAR中存在两个众所周知的问题：语义鸿沟和域偏移。语义鸿沟的产生是因为标签表示来自文本域（即语言模型），必须与视觉表示（即CNN、RNN、基于Transformer的模型）相关联。这种多模态特性意味着两个空间的语义属性并不相同。另一方面，域偏移源于训练集和测试集之间的差异，并且由于测试集未知而成为ZSAR固有的问题。解决这两个问题最有前景的方法之一是学习联合嵌入空间。因此，我们提出了一种新模型，将视频和句子编码到联合嵌入空间中，通过将视频与其自然语言描述对齐来训练模型。我们设计了一种自动负采样程序来扩充训练数据集，并生成不配对数据，即视觉外观与无关描述。我们的方法在UCF-101和Kinetics-400数据集上的多种划分配置下均取得了最先进的结果。我们的代码可在https://github.com/valterlej/cezsar获取。

### [26] [CADFit: Precise Mesh-to-CAD Program Generation with Hybrid Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01171)
*Ghadi Nehme,Eamon Whalen,Faez Ahmed*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出CADFit，一种基于混合优化的CAD重建框架，能够从网格等几何输入中恢复复杂、可编辑的CAD构造序列，并通过IoU驱动的优化和丰富的操作支持显著提升重建质量，降低无效比率。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有CAD重建方法大多局限于难以编辑的格式（如网格或Brep）或简单的草图-拉伸流水线及低复杂度数据集，无法有效恢复复杂、可编辑的CAD构造序列，亟需一种能够从几何输入中准确重建高阶CAD模型的方法。

Method: 提出CADFit框架，将重建问题形式化为基于IoU驱动的结构化CAD程序优化，通过增量拟合和验证参数化操作（包括拉伸、旋转、倒圆角、倒角等），并利用几何反馈引导优化过程。同时构建多模态流水线，结合基于图像的几何重建与CADFit，实现从图像到CAD构造序列的端到端重建。

Result: 在多个CAD基准上，CADFit在体积交并比和倒角距离上均优于最先进的网格到CAD方法，并显著降低了重建CAD程序的无效比率，尤其适用于复杂设计。

Conclusion: CADFit通过精确重建高复杂度CAD模型，为生成更丰富的数据集和推动未来基于学习的CAD逆向工程方法提供了实用基础。

Original Abstract: Despite recent progress, recovering parametric CAD construction sequences from geometric input, such as meshes or point clouds, is a key challenge for design and manufacturing, as existing CAD reconstruction and generation methods are largely restricted to difficult-to-edit formats like meshes or Breps or editable simple sketch-and-extrude pipelines and low-complexity datasets. We introduce CADFit, a hybrid optimization-based CAD reconstruction framework that recovers complex, editable CAD construction sequences from meshes by incrementally fitting and validating parametric operations using geometric feedback. Our approach is distinguished by formulating reconstruction as an IoU-driven optimization over structured CAD programs and supporting a rich set of operations, including extrusions, revolutions, fillets, and chamfers. Experiments on multiple CAD benchmarks show that CADFit outperforms state-of-the-art mesh-to-CAD methods in volumetric Intersection-over-Union and Chamfer Distance, while substantially reducing the Invalid Ratio of reconstructed CAD programs, particularly for complex designs. We further present a multimodal pipeline that enables end-to-end reconstruction of CAD construction sequences from images by combining image-based geometry reconstruction with CADFit. By enabling accurate reconstruction of higher-complexity CAD models, CADFit provides a practical foundation for generating richer datasets and advancing future learning-based approaches to CAD reverse engineering.

中文摘要翻译: 尽管近期取得了进展，但从几何输入（如网格或点云）中恢复参数化CAD构造序列仍是设计和制造领域的一项关键挑战，因为现有的CAD重建和生成方法大多局限于难以编辑的格式（如网格或Brep），或仅限于可编辑的简单草图-拉伸流水线及低复杂度数据集。本文提出了CADFit，一种基于混合优化的CAD重建框架，能够通过利用几何反馈增量式拟合和验证参数化操作，从网格中恢复复杂且可编辑的CAD构造序列。本方法的独特之处在于将重建形式化为对结构化CAD程序进行基于IoU驱动的优化，并支持丰富的操作集，包括拉伸、旋转、倒圆角和倒角。在多个CAD基准上的实验表明，CADFit在体积交并比和倒角距离上均优于最先进的网格到CAD方法，同时显著降低了重建CAD程序的无效比率，尤其对于复杂设计。我们还提出了一个多模态流水线，通过将基于图像的几何重建与CADFit相结合，实现从图像到CAD构造序列的端到端重建。通过实现高复杂度CAD模型的精确重建，CADFit为生成更丰富的数据集以及推动未来基于学习的CAD逆向工程方法提供了实用基础。

</details>


### [27] [Asymmetric Invertible Threat: Learning Reversible Privacy Defense for Face Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01217)
*Jiabei Zhang,Ziyuan Yang,Andrew Beng Jin Teoh,Yi Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出非对称可逆人脸保护方法（ARFP），通过密钥条件流形绑定、对抗性恢复感知训练与授权可逆恢复三个组件，在抵御恢复攻击的同时保持授权恢复能力，并支持篡改检测。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有对抗性隐私保护方法依赖输入空间扰动来混淆身份信息，但当攻击者学习恢复或净化映射时，保护效果会下降，因为现有防御范式无法控制可逆性。

Method: ARFP包含三个组件：1) 密钥条件流形绑定：将保护变换绑定到用户提供的密钥；2) 对抗性恢复感知训练：引入替代恢复攻击者进行对抗训练，提升对逆向净化攻击的鲁棒性；3) 授权可逆恢复：使用正确密钥支持恢复，并通过nonce提供篡改检测。

Result: 在考虑威胁模型下的广泛实验表明，ARFP在保持授权恢复效用的同时，提升了对评估的恢复攻击的抵抗能力，展示了密钥敏感的恢复行为和篡改感知能力。

Conclusion: ARFP通过非对称可逆设计有效解决了现有人脸隐私保护方法易被逆向恢复的问题，在隐私保护、密钥恢复和篡改检测之间取得了良好的平衡。

Original Abstract: Face Recognition systems are widely deployed in real-world applications, but they also raise privacy concerns due to unauthorized collection and misuse of facial data. Existing adversarial privacy protection methods rely on input-space perturbations to obfuscate identity information, yet their protection can degrade when adversaries learn restoration or purification mappings that partially invert the transformation. We study this setting as an asymmetric adversarial attack, in which reverse manipulation becomes feasible because existing defense paradigms do not control reversibility. To address this problem, we propose Asymmetric Reversible Face Protection (ARFP), a restoration-aware extension of personalized face cloaking that integrates privacy protection, keyed recovery, and tamper indication in a single framework. ARFP consists of three components: Key-Conditioned Manifold Binding, which ties the protection transformation to a user-provided key; Adversarial Restoration-Aware Training, which introduces a surrogate restoration adversary during training to improve robustness against evaluated inverse purification attacks; and Authorized Reversible Restoration, which supports recovery with the correct key while providing nonce-based tamper indication. Extensive experiments under the threat models considered in this work show that ARFP improves resistance to the evaluated restoration attacks while preserving authorized recovery utility. These results provide empirical evidence of key-sensitive recovery behavior and tamper awareness in the tested settings.

中文摘要翻译: 人脸识别系统已广泛应用于现实场景，但面部数据的未经授权收集和滥用引发了隐私问题。现有的对抗性隐私保护方法依赖输入空间扰动来混淆身份信息，然而当攻击者学习到能够部分逆转变换的恢复或净化映射时，其保护效果会下降。本文将这一设定研究为一种非对称对抗攻击，其中反向操纵变得可行，因为现有防御范式无法控制可逆性。为解决该问题，我们提出非对称可逆人脸保护方法（ARFP），这是一种面向恢复的可逆个性化人脸掩蔽扩展，将隐私保护、密钥恢复和篡改检测集成在单一框架中。ARFP由三个组件组成：密钥条件流形绑定，将保护变换与用户提供的密钥关联；对抗性恢复感知训练，在训练过程中引入替代恢复攻击者，以提升对评估的逆向净化攻击的鲁棒性；以及授权可逆恢复，支持使用正确密钥进行恢复，同时提供基于随机数的篡改检测。在本文所考虑的威胁模型下进行的大量实验表明，ARFP在保持授权恢复效用的同时，提升了对评估的恢复攻击的抵抗能力。这些结果为所测试设置下的密钥敏感恢复行为和篡改感知能力提供了经验证据。

### [28] [Visual Implicit Autoregressive Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01220)
*Pengfei Jiang,Jixiang Luo,Luxi Lin,Zhaohong Huang,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VIAR是一种基于隐式平衡层的视觉自回归建模方法，通过next-scale预测实现可控计算量与低内存占用，在ImageNet 256×256上以38.4%的参数量达到FID 2.16，并能动态调整推理计算量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有视觉自回归模型（如VAR）基于显式深层堆叠，导致每个尺度的计算量固定且高分辨率下内存膨胀，缺乏计算灵活性与部署效率。

Method: 在浅层预/后处理块之间嵌入一个隐式平衡层作为next-scale自回归生成器，采用无雅可比反向传播（Jacobian-Free Backpropagation）训练使训练内存恒定，推理时通过每尺度迭代旋钮实现计算量控制。

Result: ImageNet 256×256上FID 2.16、sFID 8.07，仅用VAR 38.4%的参数量；峰值内存从19.24 GB降至8.53 GB，吞吐量从15.16提升至32.08 images/s；零样本修复和类别条件编辑生成更锐利的细节与更平滑的边界。

Conclusion: 隐式平衡层与每尺度计算控制机制为实际可部署的视觉生成提供了高效、灵活且质量优异的解决方案，验证了隐式平衡在视觉自回归建模中的有效性。

Original Abstract: Visual Autoregressive Modeling (VAR) based on next-scale prediction achieves strong generation quality, but their explicit deep stacks fix the amount of computation per scale and inflate memory at high resolutions. We introduce Visual Implicit Autoregressive Modeling (VIAR), a next-scale autoregressive generator that embeds an implicit equilibrium layer between shallow pre/post blocks. The implicit layer is trained with Jacobian-Free Backpropagation, yielding constant training memory, while inference exposes a per-scale iteration knob that enables compute control. On ImageNet 256x256 benchmark, VIAR attains FID 2.16, and sFID 8.07 with only 38.4% parameters of VAR, matching or surpassing strong AR baselines and remaining competitive with large diffusion models. By controlling the per-scale knob, VIAR can reduce peak memory from 19.24 GB to 8.53 GB and doubles throughput from 15.16 to 32.08 images/s on a single RTX 4090, without retraining. Ablations show that fewer steps are sufficient for fixed-point iterations to converge and that VIAR consistently dominates VAR across quality efficiency operating points. In zero shot in-painting and class-conditional editing, VIAR produces sharper details and smoother boundaries while preserving global structure, validating the benefits of implicit equilibria and per-scale compute control for practical, deployable visual generation.

中文摘要翻译: 基于下一尺度预测的视觉自回归建模（VAR）取得了强大的生成质量，但其显式的深层堆叠使得每个尺度的计算量固定，并在高分辨率下导致内存膨胀。我们提出了视觉隐式自回归建模（VIAR），一种在浅层预/后处理块之间嵌入隐式平衡层的下一尺度自回归生成器。隐式层通过无雅可比反向传播训练，实现训练内存恒定，而推理时暴露每尺度迭代旋钮，允许计算量控制。在ImageNet 256×256基准上，VIAR取得了FID 2.16和sFID 8.07，仅使用VAR 38.4%的参数量，匹配或超越强自回归基线，并与大规模扩散模型保持竞争力。通过控制每尺度旋钮，VIAR可在无需重新训练的情况下，将峰值内存从19.24 GB降至8.53 GB，并将吞吐量从15.16提高到32.08 images/s（单张RTX 4090）。消融实验表明，固定点迭代在较少步骤即可收敛，且VIAR在质量-效率操作点上持续优于VAR。在零样本修复和类别条件编辑中，VIAR生成更锐利的细节和更平滑的边界，同时保持全局结构，验证了隐式平衡和每尺度计算控制对实际可部署视觉生成的益处。

### [29] [Exploring Prompt Alignment with Clinical Factors in Zero-Shot Segmentation VLMs for NSCLC Tumor Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01266)
*Suraj Pai,Thibault Heintz,Cosmin Ciausu,Marion Tonneau,Hugo Aerts,Raymond Mak*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统探究了零样本视觉语言模型（VLM）在非小细胞肺癌GTV勾画任务中的提示维度对齐行为，发现解剖位置是空间注意力的主导因素，而组织学与分期影响甚微；VoxTell在零样本设置下达到了与有监督nnUNet统计上无显著差异的Dice系数（0.613 vs 0.690），并显著优于其他零样本模型，研究建议应从Dice和提示对齐维度两方面评估分割VLM。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 零样本VLM为NSCLC的GTV勾画提供了可提示的替代方案，但控制其空间行为的提示维度尚未被充分理解，需要系统解析哪种提示信息真正驱动模型的空间注意力。

Method: 通过子提示分解（诊断、人口学、分期、解剖、通用、无关对照）、属性级扰动鲁棒性、特异性阶梯、跨病例提示交换等方法，在VoxTell上系统探测对齐方向，并以DSC、Wilcoxon符号秩检验和Benjamini-Hochberg校正进行基准对比。

Result: 解剖位置是VoxTell空间注意力的主导因素（63.4%的位置扰动导致灾难性下降）；组织学与分期替换影响极小；无关提示正确输出零分割；跨病例交换证实患者特异性条件控制（匹配DSC 0.906 vs 不匹配0.406）；VoxTell零样本平均DSC为0.613，与nnUNet（0.690，校正p=0.156）无显著差异，显著优于其他零样本模型。

Conclusion: 分割VLM不仅应通过Dice评估，还应考察其所对齐的提示维度，解剖位置是主导空间注意力的关键因素，模型更关注"看哪里"而非"看什么"。

Original Abstract: Zero-shot vision-language models (VLMs) offer a promptable alternative to task-specific training for gross tumor volume (GTV) delineation in non-small-cell lung cancer (NSCLC), but the prompt dimensions that govern their spatial behavior remain poorly understood. We study this question by probing alignment directions in VoxTell on a held-out internal NSCLC tumor dataset through sub-prompt decomposition into diagnosis, demographic, staging, anatomical, generic, and irrelevant controls; attribute-wise perturbation robustness; specificity ladders; and cross-case prompt swaps, while benchmarking against fine-tuned and zero-shot baselines using the Dice Similarity Coefficient (DSC) with Wilcoxon signed-rank tests and Benjamini-Hochberg correction. Alignment analyses revealed that anatomical location is the dominant driver of VoxTell's spatial attention: 63.4 percent of location perturbations caused catastrophic drops, prompt specificity improved from generic to full descriptions except for diagnosis-only prompts, irrelevant prompts correctly yielded zero segmentation, and cross-case prompt swaps confirmed patient-specific conditioning (matched DSC 0.906 vs. mismatched 0.406). Histology and stage substitutions had minimal effect, indicating that the model prioritizes "where to look" over "what to look for." In this context, VoxTell, operating fully zero-shot, achieved a mean DSC of 0.613, statistically indistinguishable from nnUNet (0.690, adjusted p = 0.156) and Ahmed et al. (0.675, adjusted p = 0.679), while significantly outperforming all other zero-shot models. Together, these findings argue that segmentation VLMs should be evaluated not only by Dice, but also by the prompt dimensions to which they align.

中文摘要翻译: 零样本视觉语言模型（VLM）为非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）的肿瘤大体体积（GTV）勾画提供了可提示的替代方案，无需针对特定任务进行训练，但控制其空间行为的提示维度尚不清晰。本研究通过以下方法探究这一问题：在VoxTell上对预留的内部NSCLC肿瘤数据集进行子提示分解（包括诊断、人口学、分期、解剖、通用和无关对照）、属性级扰动鲁棒性分析、特异性阶梯实验以及跨病例提示交换，同时以Dice相似系数（DSC）为指标，结合Wilcoxon符号秩检验和Benjamini-Hochberg校正，与微调和零样本基线模型进行对比。对齐分析表明，解剖位置是VoxTell空间注意力的主导驱动因素：63.4%的位置扰动导致了灾难性下降；提示特异性从通用描述提升至完整描述（仅诊断提示除外）；无关提示正确输出零分割结果；跨病例提示交换证实了患者特定条件控制（匹配DSC为0.906，不匹配为0.406）。组织学和分期替换影响甚微，表明模型更优先关注"看哪里"而非"看什么"。在此背景下，VoxTell以完全零样本方式运行，平均DSC达到0.613，与nnUNet（0.690，校正p=0.156）和Ahmed等人（0.675，校正p=0.679）无统计学显著差异，同时显著优于所有其他零样本模型。综合来看，这些发现表明，分割VLM不仅应通过Dice进行评价，还应考察其所对齐的提示维度。

</details>


### [30] [Developing a Strong Pre-Trained Base Model for Plant Leaf Disease Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01283)
*David J. Richter*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 该论文针对植物叶部病害分类领域数据集不足的问题，通过构建新数据集并基于DenseNet201架构训练出性能更优的基础模型，该模型在迁移学习中具有更快、更稳健、数据需求更少的优势。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 植物病害导致巨大产量损失，传统人工检测耗时费力；虽已有机器学习方法尤其是CNN应用于此领域，但公开数据集与训练完备模型所需的数据之间存在显著差距，现有模型性能受限于数据不足。

Method: 首先识别并筛选公开的植物叶部病害分类数据集，进行广泛基准测试；然后基于测试结果和增强适用性研究构建新数据集；最后基于DenseNet201架构训练新基础模型，并通过迁移学习进行跨数据集验证。

Result: 新构建的DenseNet201基础模型在新数据集上优于基线模型，同时在另一个新数据集的植物叶部病害分类迁移学习实验中表现更优，训练速度更快、鲁棒性更强、稳定性更高、所需数据更少。

Conclusion: 所提出的新基础模型通过迁移学习方式能够有效克服现有植物病害分类领域的数据不足问题，实现更快、更稳健、数据效率更高的模型训练。

Original Abstract: Plants, crops and their yields are essential to our very existence, but diseases and pests cause large losses every year. As such it is vital to ensure that diseases can be spotted early and treated accordingly and stopping the spread while still possible. Manual and traditional methods require personal to walk through the field and check for symptoms 'by hand'. This is very laborious and very time consuming, so ML methods have been applied as a result and they have garnered promising results. CNN models are especially efficient as they can automatically extract features from images without any manual feature construction before then feeding the features to a classifier. Datasets are largely influential to the final performance of the model. Despite the importance that datasets pose to the field, there still seems to be somewhat of a discrepancy between what is publicly available for use and what would be required to sufficiently train fully capable models. To overcome these shortcomings, as part of this thesis open datasets for the field of plant leaf disease classification have been identified as well as models that can be trained on them and extensive benchmarks have been carried out to identify their suitability. Then a new dataset was constructed based on those findings as well as on the findings of a augmentation applicability study, which will be used to train a new Base Model based on the DenseNet201 architecture, which managed to outperform the baseline model on said new dataset as well as outperforming it on plant leaf disease classification domain specific Transfer-Learning experiments on another new dataset. This new model manages to train models through Transfer-Learning (TL) faster, more robust, more stable, and with less data than general model would, overcoming a large number of issues that the field still suffers from.

中文摘要翻译: 植物、农作物及其产量对我们的生存至关重要，但病害和虫害每年都造成巨大损失。因此，及早发现病害并及时处理、在可能时阻止传播至关重要。人工和传统方法需要人员走进田地，"手工"检查症状，既费力又耗时，因此机器学习方法被引入并取得了可观的结果。CNN模型尤其高效，因为它们能从图像中自动提取特征，无需任何手动特征构建，然后将特征输入分类器。数据集对模型的最终性能影响很大。尽管数据集对该领域至关重要，但公开可用的数据集与训练出完备模型所需的数据之间仍存在一定差距。为克服这些不足，本论文识别了植物叶部病害分类领域的开放数据集以及可在其上训练的模型，并开展了广泛的基准测试以评估其适用性。随后，基于这些发现以及数据增强适用性研究的结果，构建了一个新数据集，用于训练基于DenseNet201架构的新基础模型。该模型在新数据集上的表现优于基线模型，同时在另一个新数据集上的植物叶部病害分类领域特定迁移学习实验中也取得了更优性能。新模型通过迁移学习训练出的模型比通用模型更快、更鲁棒、更稳定，且所需数据更少，克服了该领域仍面临的诸多问题。
