### [171] [Concepts Whisper While Syntax Shouts: Spectral Anti-Concentration and the Dual Geometry of Transformer Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01609)
*Pratyush Acharya,Nuraj Rimal,Habish Dhakal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现基于解嵌协方差Σ的因果内积无法实现跨语言概念传输（白化因果对齐与谱正则化无显著差异，p=0.95），但揭示了一个更普遍的现象：激活空间中概念方向在谱尾部反聚集，而静态解嵌行对比在高方差方向聚集。通过分割注入因果干预和词性标注探测，验证了Transformer可能在语境化处理中将语义内容旋转到谱安静区域，从而在减少语法干扰的前提下进行概念操控。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 检验Park等人（2024）提出的因果内积（由解嵌协方差Σ定义）是否能够实现跨语言概念传输，并探究其失败背后揭示的更广泛现象。

Method: 采用匹配谱随机化检验（matched-spectrum randomization test）评估白化因果对齐；通过SAE特征、线性探针和分割注入因果干预（split-injection causal interventions）进行分析；使用词性标注（POS-tag）探针在8个模型上进行语法编码分析。

Result: 白化因果对齐与纯谱正则化无显著差异（p=0.95）；残差流均值差向量在5个架构家族中呈现抗聚集（p<10^{-33}）；概念方向在激活空间谱尾部抗聚集，解嵌行对比在高方差方向聚集（p<10^{-4}）；分割注入干预在Gemma和Llama上验证了功能基础（Cohen's d最高1.80）；8个模型中6个的语法优先编码在高方差子空间（p<0.013），Qwen 2.5家族出现显著反转。

Conclusion: Transformer可能在语境化处理中将语义内容旋转到谱安静区域，在减少语法干扰的前提下编码和操控概念，呈现出激活空间概念方向与静态解嵌方向的"对偶几何"结构。

Original Abstract: We test whether the causal inner product of \citet{park2024linear} -- defined by the unembedding covariance $Σ$ -- enables cross-lingual concept transport. Across 17 models and 4 language pairs, a matched-spectrum randomization test finds that Whitened Causal Alignment is indistinguishable from spectral regularization alone ($p = 0.95$). However, this failure reveals a broader phenomenon: anti-concentration is observed in residual-stream difference-of-means vectors across five architecture families ($p < 10^{-33}$) and supported by SAE features (e.g., $p = 4.5 \times 10^{-19}$) and linear probes on Gemma and Llama. We discover a \emph{dual geometry}: activation-space concept directions anti-concentrate in the spectral tail, while static unembedding-row contrasts \emph{concentrate} in high-variance directions ($p < 10^{-4}$). Split-injection causal interventions support the functional basis on Gemma and Llama (Cohen's $d$ up to $1.80$), and POS-tag probing across 8 models shows syntax preferentially encodes in the high-variance subspace in 6 of 8 architectures ($p < 0.013$), with the Qwen~2.5 family showing a significant reversal consistent with architecture-specific spectral structure. These results suggest transformers may rotate semantic content into spectrally quiet regions during contextualized processing, encoding concepts where they can be manipulated with reduced grammatical disruption.

中文摘要翻译: 我们检验了由\citet{park2024linear}定义的、基于解嵌协方差$Σ$的因果内积是否能够实现跨语言概念传输。在17个模型和4个语言对上，匹配谱随机化检验发现白化因果对齐与纯谱正则化不可区分（$p = 0.95$）。然而，这一失败揭示了一个更广泛的现象：残差流均值差向量在五个架构家族中均观察到抗聚集（$p < 10^{-33}$），SAE特征（例如$p = 4.5 \times 10^{-19}$）和Gemma及Llama上的线性探针也支持这一发现。我们发现了一种\emph{对偶几何}：激活空间中的概念方向在谱尾部抗聚集，而静态解嵌行对比则\emph{聚集}在高方差方向（$p < 10^{-4}$）。分割注入因果干预在Gemma和Llama上验证了其功能基础（Cohen's $d$最高达$1.80$），对8个模型的词性标注探针显示，8个架构中有6个的语法优先编码在高方差子空间（$p < 0.013$），而Qwen~2.5系列则表现出与架构特定谱结构一致的反转。这些结果表明，Transformer可能在语境化处理过程中将语义内容旋转到谱安静区域，在减少语法干扰的前提下编码和操控概念。

### [172] [Importance-Guided Basis Selection for Low-Rank Decomposition of Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01627)
*Daniel Agyei Asante,Ernie Chang,Yang Li*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出BSI框架，通过二阶泰勒展开估计每个基被移除后的损失增量，实现低秩分解中基的重要性排序与剪枝，在数学推理基准上超越现有方法。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有低秩压缩方法（如Basel）基于重新学习到的系数大小进行启发式剪枝，忽略了损失景观的局部几何结构，可能导致剪枝决策与任务性能不一致。

Method: BSI从任务损失关于奇异值的二阶泰勒展开出发，推导基于导数的基重要性分数，结合一阶敏感性和二阶曲率量化剪枝影响；并采用Hutchinson随机探测方法适配损失曲率，设计高效的Hessian对角估计器。

Result: 在数学推理基准上的实验表明，BSI持续优于最先进的低秩分解基线方法，尤其在深度压缩下表现突出。理论分析提供了损失增量上界、Hessian对角估计误差传播、方差表征、样本复杂度保证等结果。

Conclusion: BSI是一个 principled 的低秩压缩框架，通过直接估计基剪枝的损失影响而非启发式准则，实现了更优的压缩-性能权衡。

Original Abstract: Low-rank decomposition is a compelling approach for compressing large language models, but its effectiveness hinges on selecting which singular-vector bases to retain for a target task. Existing methods such as Basel adapt singular-value coefficients on downstream data and prune bases with small re-learned magnitudes, a heuristic that can be misaligned with task performance because it ignores the local geometry of the loss landscape. We present Basis Selection with Importance (BSI), a principled low-rank compression framework that ranks and prunes bases by directly estimating the expected loss increase incurred when each basis is removed. BSI derives a derivative-based importance score from a second-order Taylor expansion of the task loss with respect to singular values, combining first-order sensitivity and second-order curvature to quantify pruning impact. To make this criterion practical for LLMs, we develop an efficient Hessian-diagonal estimator by adapting the Hutchinson randomized-probing method to loss curvature with symmetric parameter perturbations. We provide a comprehensive theoretical analysis, including loss-increase bounds under basis pruning, explicit propagation of Hessian-diagonal estimation error into these bounds, variance characterization tied to the Hessian spectrum, high-probability sample-complexity guarantees for achieving a target estimation accuracy, and guidance on perturbation intensity. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that BSI consistently outperforms state-of-the-art low-rank decomposition baselines, with especially strong improvements under deep compression.

中文摘要翻译: 低秩分解是压缩大型语言模型的一种引人注目的方法，但其有效性取决于为目标任务选择保留哪些奇异向量基。现有方法如Basel在下游数据上调整奇异值系数，并剪枝具有较小重新学习幅度的基，这是一种启发式方法，可能因忽略损失景观的局部几何结构而与任务性能不一致。我们提出BSI（基于重要性的基选择），一个基于原则的低秩压缩框架，通过直接估计每个基被移除时预期损失增量来对基进行排序和剪枝。BSI从任务损失关于奇异值的二阶泰勒展开推导出基于导数的基重要性分数，结合一阶敏感性和二阶曲率来量化剪枝影响。为使该准则对大型语言模型实用，我们通过将Hutchinson随机探测方法适配到具有对称参数扰动的损失曲率，开发了一个高效的Hessian对角估计器。我们提供了全面的理论分析，包括基剪枝下的损失增量上界、Hessian对角估计误差向这些上界的显式传播、与Hessian谱相关的方差表征、实现目标估计精度的高概率样本复杂度保证，以及扰动强度的指导。在数学推理基准上的大量实验表明，BSI持续优于最先进的低秩分解基线方法，尤其在深度压缩下表现突出。

</details>


### [173] [Prescriptive Scaling Laws for Data Constrained Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01640)
*Justin Lovelace,Christian Belardi,Srivatsa Kundurthy,Shriya Sudhakar,Kilian Q. Weinberger*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种适用于数据受限场景的缩放定律，通过引入简单的加性过拟合惩罚项来建模重复训练下的额外损失，并据此给出计算最优分配建议：在数据有限时，增加模型容量比重复使用数据更有效。此外，强权重衰减可将过拟合系数降低约70%，为数据受限场景下使用更大权重衰减提供了理论解释。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有的Chinchilla缩放定律假设每个训练token都是唯一的，无法有效指导数据受限场景下的预训练决策。随着高质量数据的可用性增速落后于计算资源的增长，如何从有限数据中提取最大价值成为核心挑战。

Method: 提出一种带单一参数的缩放定律，在原有损失函数基础上增加一个加性过拟合惩罚项来建模重复训练导致的额外损失。该形式将过拟合隔离在单一系数中，便于跨训练配置进行直接比较。

Result: 1）该缩放定律能准确描述重复训练下模型的行为；2）在数据受限场景下，超过一定阈值后重复使用数据适得其反，应将计算资源用于增加模型容量；3）强权重衰减（λ=1.0）可将过拟合系数降低约70%，解释了为什么数据受限场景下最优权重衰减比标准做法大一个数量级。

Conclusion: 本文提出的缩放定律为数据受限场景下的计算最优分配提供了新的定性建议，并通过单一参数形式实现了训练配置间的直接比较。强权重衰减能显著降低过拟合系数，为实际训练中采用更大权重衰减提供了理论依据。

Original Abstract: Training compute is increasingly outpacing the availability of high-quality data. This shifts the central challenge from optimal compute allocation to extracting maximum value from limited data. The widely adopted Chinchilla scaling law assumes every training token is unique. This limits its ability to guide pretraining decisions in data-constrained regimes. We model the excess loss under repetition with a simple additive overfitting penalty and find that it accurately describes model behavior. Our scaling law yields qualitatively new compute-optimal allocation advice. Beyond a point, further repetition is counterproductive and compute is better spent on model capacity. We show that following our law's recommended configuration improves performance in data-constrained regimes. Finally, because our one-parameter form isolates overfitting in a single coefficient, it enables direct comparison across training configurations. As a case study, we show that strong weight decay ($λ=1.0$) reduces this coefficient by approximately 70%, providing a scaling-law explanation for recent findings that optimal weight decay in data-constrained regimes is an order of magnitude larger than standard practice.

中文摘要翻译: 训练计算资源的增长速度正日益超过高质量数据的可用性。这使得核心挑战从最优计算分配转变为从有限数据中提取最大价值。广泛采用的Chinchilla缩放定律假设每个训练token都是唯一的，这限制了其在数据受限场景下指导预训练决策的能力。我们通过一个简单的加性过拟合惩罚项来建模重复训练下的额外损失，并发现该模型能够准确描述模型行为。我们的缩放定律提供了具有定性差异的计算最优分配建议：超过某个阈值后，进一步重复使用数据会适得其反，计算资源应更好地用于增加模型容量。我们证明，遵循我们定律推荐配置能够在数据受限场景下提升性能。最后，由于我们的单参数形式将过拟合隔离在单一系数中，它能够实现跨训练配置的直接比较。作为案例研究，我们表明强权重衰减（λ=1.0）可将该系数降低约70%，从而为近期发现的数据受限场景下最优权重衰减比标准做法大一个数量级这一现象提供了缩放定律层面的解释。

</details>


### [174] [AI Alignment via Incentives and Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01643)
*Rohit Agarwal,Joshua Lin,Mark Braverman,Elad Hazan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将AI对齐问题建模为执法经济学中的威慑与执行模型，提出对齐是一个不动点问题：更强的惩罚可能抑制求解器不当行为，但也会降低审计者的检查动机。文章形式化了一个双智能体模型，将奖励设计视为双层优化问题，并通过基于bandit的外环搜索方法，在LLM编码流水线上验证了自适应奖励可以维持有效的监督压力并提升对齐效果。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统AI对齐方法将不当行为视为外部失败，忽视了智能体对激励的理性响应。本文受法律与经济学的威慑模型启发，将求解器的不当行为视为策略性选择——求解器会权衡违规收益与被检测概率及惩罚严重性，因此对齐需要从激励机制设计角度重新审视。

Method: 提出一个双智能体（求解器-审计者）形式化模型，主理人根据联合修正结果分配奖励，诱导求解器行为与审计者监控策略；将奖励设计建模为双层优化问题，并设计基于bandit的外环搜索过程，利用带噪声的交互反馈搜索最优奖励配置。

Result: 在LLM编码流水线实验中，自适应奖励配置相比静态手工设计的奖励，能够维持有效的监督压力，显著减少幻觉性的错误尝试，提升主理人期望的对齐结果。

Conclusion: AI对齐本质上是一个激励设计问题，需要将奖励视为影响行为均衡的工具而非对语义正确性的直接评判；求解器-审计者的互动结构暴露了更丰富的修正信号，合理设计奖励可以改善对齐效果。

Original Abstract: We study AI alignment through the lens of law-and-economics models of deterrence and enforcement. In these models, misconduct is not treated as an external failure, but as a strategic response to incentives: an actor weighs the gain from violation against the probability of detection and the severity of punishment. We argue that the same logic arises naturally in agentic AI pipelines. A solver may benefit from producing a persuasive but incorrect answer, hiding uncertainty, or exploiting spurious shortcuts, while an auditor or verifier must decide whether costly monitoring is worthwhile. Alignment is therefore a fixed-point problem: stronger penalties may deter solver misbehavior, but they can also reduce the auditor's incentive to inspect, since auditing then mainly incurs cost on a population that appears increasingly aligned.
  This perspective also changes what should count as a post-training signal. Standard feedback often attaches reward to the final answer alone, but a solver-auditor pipeline exposes the full correction event: whether the solver erred, whether the auditor inspected, whether the error was caught, and whether oversight incentives remained active. We formalize this interaction in a two-agent model in which a principal chooses rewards over joint correction outcomes, inducing both solver behavior and auditor monitoring. Reward design is therefore a bilevel optimization problem: rewards are judged not by their immediate semantic meaning, but by the behavioral equilibrium they induce. We propose a bandit-based outer-loop procedure for searching over reward profiles using noisy interaction feedback. Experiments on an LLM coding pipeline show that adaptive reward profiles can maintain useful oversight pressure and improve principal-aligned outcomes relative to static hand-designed rewards, including a substantial reduction in hallucinated incorrect attempts.

中文摘要翻译: 我们从法律与经济学的威慑和执行模型视角研究AI对齐问题。在这些模型中，不当行为不被视为外部失败，而是对激励的策略性响应：行为者权衡违规收益与被检测概率及惩罚严重性。我们认为，同样的逻辑自然地出现在智能体AI流水线中。求解器可能受益于生成有说服力但不正确的答案、隐藏不确定性或利用虚假捷径，而审计者或验证者必须决定昂贵的监控是否值得。因此，对齐是一个不动点问题：更强的惩罚可能抑制求解器的不当行为，但也会降低审计者的检查动机，因为审计主要对看起来越来越对齐的群体施加成本。
  这一视角也改变了什么应被视为后训练信号。标准反馈通常仅将奖励附加到最终答案上，但求解器-审计者流水线暴露了完整的修正事件：求解器是否出错、审计者是否检查、错误是否被捕获以及监督激励是否保持活跃。我们在一个双智能体模型中形式化了这一交互，其中主理人根据联合修正结果选择奖励，诱导求解器行为和审计者监控。因此，奖励设计是一个双层优化问题：奖励不是通过其直接语义意义，而是通过它们诱导的行为均衡来评判。我们提出了一个基于bandit的外环流程，利用带噪声的交互反馈搜索奖励配置。在LLM编码流水线上的实验表明，相比静态手工设计的奖励，自适应奖励配置可以维持有效的监督压力并改善主理人对齐的结果，包括大幅减少幻觉性的错误尝试。

</details>


### [175] [Geospatial foundation-model embeddings improve population estimation unevenly across space and scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01650)
*Wenbin Zhang,Eimear Cleary,Francisco Rowe,Somnath Chaudhuri,Maksym Bondarenko,Shengjie Lai,Andrew J. Tatem*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文评估了地理空间基础模型（PDFM）在次国家级人口估计中的表现，发现其相比传统地理空间协变量可提升预测精度（中位减少20.1%未解释方差），但在空间尺度迁移时存在局限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统人口制图依赖手工构建的地理空间协变量（如聚落范围、夜间灯光等），这些数据需要跨尺度和地理区域进行组装与协调，过程繁琐且存在数据稀疏、陈旧或空间分辨率粗糙的问题。因此，探索地理空间基础模型作为替代方案具有重要意义。

Method: 使用人口动态基础模型（PDFM）的嵌入表示，替代传统手工构建的地理空间协变量，对巴西、尼日利亚和美国进行次国家级人口估计，并在地理结构化的验证框架下与基线方法进行比较。

Result: PDFM将未解释方差中位减少20.1%（IQR: 10.0-33.2%），KL散度降低23.2%（9.2-26.2%）；但在空间尺度迁移中灵活性不如传统协变量，且在地理空间协变量对聚落背景描述较弱的区域（如较大且欠发达的次国家级区域）优势更明显。

Conclusion: 地理空间基础模型的地点表征能够改善数据匮乏地区的人口估计，但其优势在空间尺度不匹配时会可预测地失效，揭示了当前地理空间AI的一个根本性局限。

Original Abstract: Reliable subnational population estimates are essential for applications, yet remain difficult where censuses are sparse, outdated or spatially coarse. Existing population-mapping workflows rely on hand-built geospatial covariates, such as settlement extent, night-time lights, and environmental conditions, which must be assembled and harmonised across scales and geographies. Geospatial foundation models offer an alternative by learning reusable representations of place from more multifaceted and heterogeneous data sources. Here, we benchmark Population Dynamics Foundation Model (PDFM) embeddings against the harmonised geospatial covariates for subnational population estimation in Brazil, Nigeria and the United States. Under geographically structured validation, PDFM increased predictive fit by a median of 20.1% (IQR: 10.0-33.2%, across country-model comparisons) reduction in unexplained variance, and reduced Kullback-Leibler divergence by 23.2% (9.2-26.2%). However, these gains were uneven. PDFM was most advantageous where the geospatial covariates weakly characterised settlement context, such as larger and less-developed subnational areas. Moreover, PDFM performance was scale-coupled with embeddings providing less flexible transfer across spatial aggregations than geospatial covariates. These findings showed that geospatial foundation-model representations of place can improve population estimation in data poor settings, but their benefits break down predictably under spatial scale mismatch, revealing a fundamental limitation of current geospatial AI.

中文摘要翻译: 可靠的次国家级人口估计对应用至关重要，但在人口普查数据稀疏、过时或空间分辨率粗糙的地区仍然难以实现。现有的人口制图工作流程依赖手工构建的地理空间协变量，如聚落范围、夜间灯光和环境条件，这些数据需要跨尺度和地理区域进行组装与协调。地理空间基础模型通过学习来自更多样化和异质性数据源的可重用地点表征，提供了一种替代方案。本文在巴西、尼日利亚和美国对人口动态基础模型（PDFM）嵌入与统一地理空间协变量进行了次国家级人口估计的基准测试。在地理结构化的验证下，PDFM将预测拟合优度中位提升了20.1%（IQR: 10.0-33.2%，跨国家-模型比较的未解释方差减少），并将KL散度降低了23.2%（9.2-26.2%）。然而，这些增益并不均衡。PDFM在地理空间协变量对聚落背景描述较弱的区域（如较大且欠发达的次国家级区域）最具优势。此外，PDFM的性能呈现尺度耦合特性，其嵌入在空间聚合间的迁移灵活性不如地理空间协变量。这些发现表明，地理空间基础模型的地点表征可以改善数据匮乏地区的人口估计，但其优势在空间尺度不匹配时会可预测地失效，揭示了当前地理空间AI的一个根本性局限。

### [176] [Towards Efficient and Expressive Offline RL via Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01663)
*Sungyoung Lee,Dohyeong Kim,Eshan Balachandar,Zelal Su Mustafaoglu,Keshav Pingali*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FAN是一种高效的离线强化学习算法，通过单次流策略迭代和单高斯噪声样本实现行为正则化，在保持高性能的同时大幅降低计算成本。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于流策略和分布性评论家的离线RL算法性能优秀但计算开销极大，流策略需迭代采样生成动作，分布性评论家需多样本计算价值，亟需在保持高性能的前提下提升效率。

Method: 提出Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning (FAN)，核心是行为正则化技术，仅需单次流策略迭代生成动作，且分布性评论家仅需单高斯噪声样本估计价值；同时提供了收敛性和性能边界的理论分析。

Result: 在机器人操作和运动控制任务上，FAN达到了最先进的性能，同时显著缩短了训练和推理时间；理论分析证明了简化设计不仅提升效率，还带来了更优的任务性能。

Conclusion: 单次流策略迭代和单噪声样本的简化设计可兼顾离线RL的高性能和高效性，为实际应用提供了可行方案。

Original Abstract: We propose Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning (FAN), a highly efficient and high-performing offline reinforcement learning (RL) algorithm. Recent work has shown that expressive flow policies and distributional critics improve offline RL performance, but at a high computational cost. Specifically, flow policies require iterative sampling to produce a single action, and distributional critics require computation over multiple samples (e.g., quantiles) to estimate value. To address these inefficiencies while maintaining high performance, we introduce FAN. Our method employs a behavior regularization technique that utilizes only a single flow policy iteration and requires only a single Gaussian noise sample for distributional critics. Our theoretical analysis of convergence and performance bounds demonstrates that these simplifications not only improve efficiency but also lead to superior task performance. Experiments on robotic manipulation and locomotion tasks demonstrate that FAN achieves state-of-the-art performance while significantly reducing both training and inference runtimes. We release our code at https://github.com/brianlsy98/FAN.

中文摘要翻译: 我们提出了Flow-Anchored Noise-conditioned Q-Learning（FAN），一种高效且高性能的离线强化学习（RL）算法。近期研究表明，表达性强的流策略和分布性评论家能够提升离线RL性能，但代价是极高的计算成本。具体而言，流策略需要迭代采样才能生成单个动作，而分布性评论家则需要基于多个样本（如分位数）来估计价值。为了解决这些效率问题同时保持高性能，我们引入了FAN。该方法采用了一种行为正则化技术，仅需单次流策略迭代，且分布性评论家仅需单个高斯噪声样本。我们对收敛性和性能边界的理论分析表明，这些简化不仅提升了效率，还带来了更优的任务性能。在机器人操作和运动控制任务上的实验证明，FAN在达到最先进性能的同时，显著降低了训练和推理的运行时间。我们开源的代码位于 https://github.com/brianlsy98/FAN。

### [177] [Benchmarking Single-Pose Docking, Consensus Rescoring, and Supervised ML on the LIT-PCBA Library: A Critical Evaluation of DiffDock, AutoDock-GPU, GNINA, and DiffDock-NMDN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01681)
*Youssef Abo-Dahab,Xiaoiang Xiang,Xiaoiang Xiang,Xiaoiang Xiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文系统评估了传统对接方法和AI工具在真实虚拟筛选基准上的表现，发现经典方法与机器学习重排序的组合（AutoDock-GNINA + 监督学习）效果最优，但即使最佳方案在现实基准上的早期富集率仍较有限。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有AI对接工具如DiffDock和NMDN在标准基准上表现强劲，但它们在基于真实实验数据的数据集上的实际效用尚不清楚。论文旨在通过大规模真实基准评估，揭示不同对接与评分方法在实际虚拟筛选中的真实表现。

Method: 在LIT-PCBA库（15个靶点，578,295个配体-靶点对）上，使用AutoDock-GPU和DiffDock进行构象生成，然后用GNINA和NMDN进行重评分；进一步评估基于排序的共识策略和基于对接特征训练的监督机器学习模型。

Result: AutoDock-GNINA是表现最佳的单方法（中位EF1% = 2.14）；DiffDock方法整体逊色，尤其在OPRK1等挑战性靶点上；监督ML重排序带来最大提升（中位EF1% = 4.49，比AutoDock-GNINA提高110%）；精心设计的共识排序提高了鲁棒性但未超越最佳单方法。

Conclusion: 没有任何单一对接方法能跨靶点占优；经严格验证的、结合监督重排序的经典+ML混合方案当前最具实际价值，但即使最佳工作流在现实基准上的早期富集能力也仅为中等水平。

Original Abstract: Virtual screening performance depends heavily on the chosen docking and scoring methods. Recent AI-based tools such as DiffDock and NMDN have reported strong benchmark results, but their practical utility on realistic, experimentally-derived datasets remains unclear. Here we perform a large-scale evaluation on the LIT-PCBA library (15 targets, 578,295 ligand-target pairs with experimentally confirmed actives and inactives). We compare AutoDock-GPU and DiffDock for pose generation, followed by rescoring with GNINA and NMDN. We further evaluate rank-based consensus strategies and supervised machine learning models trained on docking features.
  GNINA rescoring of AutoDock-GPU poses (AutoDock-GNINA) emerged as the strongest single method with a median EF1% of 2.14. DiffDock-based approaches underperformed relative to AutoDock-GNINA, particularly on challenging targets such as OPRK1. Carefully designed consensus ranking improved robustness but did not surpass the best single scorer. Supervised ML re-ranking delivered the largest gains, achieving a median EF1% of 4.49 (+110% over AutoDock-GNINA).
  Our results highlight that even the best classical+ML hybrid workflows provide only modest early enrichment on realistic benchmarks. We conclude that no single docking method dominates across targets and that rigorously validated, cost-effective combinations with supervised re-ranking currently offer the most practical value for virtual screening.

中文摘要翻译: 虚拟筛选的性能在很大程度上取决于所选的对接和评分方法。近年来，诸如DiffDock和NMDN等基于AI的工具在标准基准上报告了强劲的结果，但它们在基于真实实验数据的实用数据集上的效用仍不明确。本文在LIT-PCBA库（15个靶点，578,295个配体-靶点对，包含实验确认的活性和非活性分子）上开展了大规模评估。我们比较了AutoDock-GPU和DiffDock在构象生成方面的表现，随后使用GNINA和NMDN进行重评分。我们还进一步评估了基于排序的共识策略以及基于对接特征训练的监督机器学习模型。结果显示，对AutoDock-GPU构象使用GNINA重评分（AutoDock-GNINA）是最强的单一方法，中位EF1%为2.14。基于DiffDock的方法整体表现逊于AutoDock-GNINA，尤其在OPRK1等挑战性靶点上。精心设计的共识排序提高了鲁棒性，但未超越最佳单一评分器。监督机器学习重排序带来了最大提升，中位EF1%达到4.49（较AutoDock-GNINA提升110%）。我们的研究结果强调，即使是最佳的经典+机器学习混合工作流在现实基准上也仅能提供中等程度的早期富集。我们得出结论：没有任何单一对接方法能在所有靶点上占据主导地位，而经过严格验证、结合监督重排序的高性价比组合方案目前为虚拟筛选提供了最具实际价值的选择。

</details>


### [178] [Probe-Geometry Alignment: Erasing the Cross-Sequence Memorization Signature Below Chance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01699)
*Anamika Paul Rupa,Anietie Andy*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现大语言模型的行为遗忘会留下可被对抗探针恢复的内部痕迹，证明这种记忆保留是真实、因果可分离且具有特定表征机制的，并提出了一种名为探针几何对齐（PGA）的手术级擦除方法，能在无需可衡量能力损失的情况下将跨序列记忆签名降至随机猜测水平以下。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有研究表明，大语言模型的"行为遗忘"（即通过微调让模型不再输出某些记忆内容）实际上并未真正抹去内部表征中的记忆痕迹，这些痕迹可被对抗性探针恢复。因此，作者希望系统地表征这些记忆保留在模型内部的何处、其性质如何，并探索能否在不损害模型能力的前提下将其精准移除。

Method: 提出探针几何对齐（Probe-Geometry Alignment, PGA）方法：首先使用留一法跨序列探针（leave-one-out cross-sequence probe）检测记忆签名是否在留出序列上泛化；然后沿着探针的实时读出方向对每一层的激活进行对齐操作，从而手术级擦除记忆签名。针对重新拟合攻击者，进一步提出对抗性PGA扩展，在每一记忆相关深度击败重新训练的探针。

Result: 1）跨序列记忆签名真实且稳定：在Pythia-70M、GPT-2 medium、Mistral-7B上分别有+0.32、+0.19、+0.30的间隙；2）探针方向与回忆行为因果可分：投影去除签名后局部签名从+0.44降至-0.19，而行为回忆几乎不变；3）自然记忆与微调注入秘密是两种表征上不同的机制；4）PGA在四个尺度上将跨序列探针降至随机猜测以下（toy depth-4: 0.17; Pythia-70M: 0.07; Mistral-7B: 0.45; GPT-2 medium: 0.06）；5）对抗性PGA在击败重新拟合探针的同时，五个零样本能力基准平均准确率变化仅+0.2个百分点，每任务变化在2.8个百分点以内。

Conclusion: 跨序列签名是预训练表征中一种真实、因果可分离、机制特定的属性，可以通过每层仅一个秩一的干预在无需可衡量能力成本的情况下将其降至随机猜测水平以下。

Original Abstract: Recent attacks show that behavioural unlearning of large language models leaves internal traces recoverable by adversarial probes. We characterise where this retention lives and show it can be surgically removed without measurable capability cost. Our central protocol is a leave-one-out cross-sequence probe that tests whether a memorisation signature generalises across held-out sequences. The signature is real and consistent across scale: memorisation-specific gaps of +0.32, +0.19, +0.30 on Pythia-70M, GPT-2 medium, and Mistral-7B; on Pythia-70M, the random-initialisation control collapses to -0.04 at the deepest layer where the pretrained signature peaks. The probe direction is causally separable from recall -- projecting it out collapses the signature locally (+0.44 -> -0.19) while behavioural recall barely changes -- and a probe trained on naturally memorised content does not classify fine-tuning-injected secrets, marking two representationally distinct regimes. We then introduce probe-geometry alignment (PGA), a surgical erasure that aligns activations along the probe's live readout direction at each depth. PGA drives the cross-sequence probe below random chance at all four scales tested (toy depth-4: 0.17; Pythia-70M: 0.07; Mistral-7B: 0.45; GPT-2 medium: 0.06 via MD-PGA k=2) and remains robust to six adversarial probe variants. Against a re-fitting attacker who trains a fresh probe on PGA-treated activations, we extend PGA adversarially, defeating the re-fit probe at every memorisation-relevant depth while preserving five zero-shot capability benchmarks within 2.8 percentage points per task (mean Δacc = +0.2pp). The cross-sequence signature is a real, causally separable, regime-specific property of pretrained representations -- removable below chance with a single rank-one intervention per depth at no measurable capability cost.

中文摘要翻译: 近期攻击表明，大语言模型的行为遗忘会留下可被对抗探针恢复的内部痕迹。本文刻画了这种记忆保留所在的部位，并证明它可以在无需可衡量能力成本的情况下被手术级移除。我们的核心协议是一种留一法跨序列探针，用于检测记忆签名是否在留出序列上泛化。该签名是真实的且跨尺度一致：在Pythia-70M、GPT-2 medium和Mistral-7B上，记忆特定的间隙分别为+0.32、+0.19、+0.30；在Pythia-70M上，随机初始化的对照在最深层（预训练签名峰值所在处）降至-0.04。探针方向与回忆行为因果可分——将其投影出去可使局部签名从+0.44降至-0.19，而行为回忆几乎不变——并且，在自然记忆内容上训练的探针无法分类微调注入的秘密，标志着两种表征上不同的机制。随后，我们提出探针几何对齐（PGA），一种手术级擦除方法，在每个深度将激活沿探针的实时读出方向对齐。PGA在所有四个测试尺度上（toy depth-4: 0.17；Pythia-70M: 0.07；Mistral-7B: 0.45；GPT-2 medium: 0.06，通过MD-PGA k=2）将跨序列探针降至随机猜测以下，并且对六种对抗性探针变体保持鲁棒性。针对一个重新拟合攻击者（其在PGA处理后的激活上训练新探针），我们对抗性地扩展PGA，在每一记忆相关深度击败重新拟合探针，同时将五个零样本能力基准维持在每任务2.8个百分点以内（平均Δacc = +0.2pp）。跨序列签名是预训练表征中一种真实、因果可分离、机制特定的属性——通过每层单个秩一的干预即可在无需可衡量能力成本的情况下将其降至随机猜测以下。

</details>


### [179] [Robust Linear Dueling Bandits with Post-serving Context under Unknown Delays and Adversarial Corruptions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01752)
*Youngmin Oh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为 \term 的算法，用于解决易变环境中带有后服务上下文、延迟反馈和对抗性损坏的线性决斗老虎机问题，理论上实现了延迟机制无关的遗憾界 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(d(\sqrt{T} + \mathcal{C} + \mathcal{D}))$，并证明损坏与延迟之间呈加性而非乘性关系。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有线性决斗老虎机研究通常假设反馈即时且环境稳定，但在实际应用中（如在线推荐、广告投放），反馈常存在随机或对抗性延迟，且可能遭受对抗性损坏，同时存在后服务上下文（post-serving contexts）这一复杂因素。现有方法在处理这些挑战时性能严重退化，亟需一种能同时应对延迟、损坏和后服务上下文的统一算法。

Method: 提出 \term 算法，包含两个核心组件：(1) 从服务前信息预测后服务上下文的学习近似器；(2) 自适应加权策略，通过对特征向量进行裁剪，同时缓解损坏观测和延迟观测的影响。

Result: 在标准正则性条件和参数化后服务映射下，算法达到遗憾上界 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(d(\sqrt{T} + \mathcal{C} + \mathcal{D}))$，其中 $\mathcal{D}$ 刻画延迟复杂度。分析表明损坏与延迟的代价呈加性结构，避免了先前工作中常见的乘性退化。此外，建立了几乎匹配的下界（在无后服务上下文的对抗延迟场景中仅差 $\sqrt{d}$ 因子）。

Conclusion: \term 算法在存在后服务上下文、延迟反馈和对抗性损坏的易变环境中实现了延迟机制无关的最优遗憾性能，其加性代价结构表明损坏和延迟对算法性能的影响是解耦的，为实际鲁棒推荐系统提供了理论保障。

Original Abstract: We study linear dueling bandits in volatile environments characterized by the simultaneous presence of post-serving contexts, delayed feedback, and adversarial corruption. Feedback is subject to unknown stochastic or adversarial delays and a cumulative corruption budget $\mathcal{C}$. To address these challenges, we propose \term, which integrates a learned approximator that predicts post-serving contexts from pre-serving information. It further employs an adaptive weighting strategy that clips feature vectors to mitigate the impact of corrupted and delayed observations simultaneously. Under standard regularity conditions and a parametric post-serving mapping, we rigorously establish that our algorithm is delay-regime-agnostic, achieving a regret upper bound of $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(d(\sqrt{T} + \mathcal{C} + \mathcal{D}))$, where $d$ is the total feature dimension and $\mathcal{D}$ encapsulates the delay complexity. Crucially, our analysis reveals an additive cost structure between corruption and delay, avoiding the multiplicative degradation typical of prior works. We further establish lower bounds that nearly match our upper bounds up to a $\sqrt{d}$ factor for adversarial delays in the absence of post-serving contexts.

中文摘要翻译: 我们研究易变环境中的线性决斗老虎机问题，这类环境的特征是同时存在后服务上下文、延迟反馈和对抗性损坏。反馈受到未知的随机或对抗性延迟以及累积损坏预算 $\mathcal{C}$ 的影响。为应对这些挑战，我们提出 \term 算法，该算法集成一个学习近似器，用于从服务前信息预测后服务上下文。此外，它采用一种自适应加权策略，通过裁剪特征向量来同时减轻损坏观测和延迟观测的影响。在标准正则性条件和参数化后服务映射下，我们严格证明该算法具有延迟机制无关性，实现了 $\widetilde{\mathcal{O}}(d(\sqrt{T} + \mathcal{C} + \mathcal{D}))$ 的遗憾上界，其中 $d$ 是总特征维度，$\mathcal{D}$ 概括了延迟复杂度。关键的是，我们的分析揭示了损坏与延迟之间呈加性代价结构，避免了先前工作中典型的乘性退化。我们进一步给出了下界，在无后服务上下文的对抗延迟场景中，该下界与我们的上界几乎匹配，仅相差 $\sqrt{d}$ 因子。

### [180] [Mitigating Multimodal LLMs Hallucinations via Relevance Propagation at Inference Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01766)
*Itai Allouche,Joseph Keshet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了LIME框架，一种无需训练、在推理时增强多模态大语言模型对感知输入依赖的方法，通过LRP量化token贡献并更新键值表征，有效减少幻觉现象。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 多模态大语言模型在推理时存在模态利用不平衡的问题，文本token主导导致模型过度依赖语言先验而产生幻觉，需要一种无需训练的方法来增强模型对感知输入的利用。

Method: 提出LIME框架：1）利用层相关性传播（LRP）量化每个token对输出的贡献；2）定义基于相关性的目标函数，鼓励模型增加对感知输入的依赖；3）在推理时通过更新模型的键值（KV）表征来优化该目标，无需修改模型参数或额外训练数据。

Result: 在多个视觉和音频多模态基准上，LIME一致减少了幻觉并增强了多模态接地能力，同时保持了生成质量；进一步分析表明该方法增加了模态贡献并产生了更局部化和语义对齐的相关性模式。

Conclusion: LIME是一种有效的无需训练的推理时增强框架，能够通过显式增强模态使用来缓解多模态大语言模型的幻觉问题，且不牺牲生成质量。

Original Abstract: Multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have revolutionized the landscape of AI, demonstrating impressive capabilities in tackling complex vision and audio-language tasks. However, a critical challenge remains: these models often suffer from hallucinations, generating outputs that diverge from the provided perceptual inputs. This tendency stems from an inherent imbalance in modality utilization during inference, where the dominance of textual tokens undermines the potential of perceptual inputs. As a result, the model frequently resorts to textual language priors at the expense of grounded evidence. To tackle this issue, we propose Learning Inference-time Modality Enhancement (LIME), a training-free framework designed to bolster multimodal grounding by explicitly enhancing modality usage during decoding. LIME leverages Layer-wise Relevance Propagation (LRP) to quantify token-level contributions and defines a relevance-based objective that promotes increased reliance on perceptual inputs. This objective is enforced through inference-time updates to the model's key-value representations, without modifying model parameters or requiring additional training data. We evaluate LIME across multiple multimodal benchmarks in both vision and audio domains, demonstrating consistent reductions in hallucinations and enhanced grounding while preserving generation quality. Further analysis shows that LIME increases modality contribution and produces more localized and semantically aligned relevance patterns.

中文摘要翻译: 多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）已经革新了人工智能的格局，在解决复杂的视觉和音频-语言任务方面展现出了令人印象深刻的能力。然而，一个关键挑战仍然存在：这些模型常常出现幻觉，生成偏离所提供的感知输入的输出。这一趋势源于推理过程中模态利用固有的不平衡，文本token的主导地位削弱了感知输入的潜力。因此，模型经常以牺牲基于证据的输入为代价，转而依赖文本语言先验。为了解决这个问题，我们提出学习推理时模态增强（LIME），这是一个无需训练的框架，通过在解码过程中显式增强模态使用来加强多模态接地。LIME利用层相关性传播（LRP）量化token级别的贡献，并定义一个基于相关性的目标，以促进对感知输入的更大依赖。这一目标通过推理时对模型键值表征的更新来实现，无需修改模型参数或额外训练数据。我们在视觉和音频领域的多个多模态基准上评估了LIME，结果表明该方法在保持生成质量的同时，一致地减少了幻觉并增强了接地能力。进一步分析显示，LIME增加了模态贡献，并产生了更局部化和语义对齐的相关性模式。

### [181] [Beyond ECE: Calibrated Size Ratio, Risk Assessment, and Confidence-Weighted Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01796)
*Fernando Martin-Maroto,Nabil Abderrahaman,Gonzalo G. de Polavieja*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出现有的置信度校准评估指标ECE存在缺陷（即使存在严重过度自信风险时仍可能很小），提出了新的评估指标CSR（校准尺寸比）及风险概率P_risk，并引入置信度加权准确率cwA及其扩展指标cwAUC来补充评估置信度的判别能力。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有评估校准的主流指标ECE存在严重缺陷：在线性度量下即使存在任意大的过度自信风险，ECE仍可能保持很小的值，无法真实反映校准问题。因此需要更鲁棒、更具解释性的校准评估指标。

Method: 1) 提出CSR（Calibrated Size Ratio）指标，完美校准下取值为1，并基于此导出风险概率P_risk量化过度自信的统计证据；2) 提出置信度加权准确率cwA作为评估置信度判别能力的自然补充指标，并将置信度加权扩展到所有标准分类指标；3) 证明置信度加权的AUC（cwAUC）能捕获校准信息而经典AUC不能。

Result: 在多种合成置信度分布（多种可控校准曲线）及15个真实数据集（含/不含事后校准）上的实验表明，CSR在所有测试条件下均达到接近完美的敏感性和特异性。

Conclusion: CSR相比ECE能更可靠地检测过度自信风险，且置信度加权指标（cwA、cwAUC等）能有效补充校准评估中缺失的判别能力维度，为置信度校准评估提供了更完善的框架。

Original Abstract: Confidence calibration has been dominated by the Expected Calibration Error (ECE), a linear metric that counts calibration offset equally regardless of the confidence level at which it occurs. We show that ECE can remain small even under arbitrarily large overconfidence risk, so we propose Calibrated Size Ratio (CSR) instead, an interpretable metric that equals 1 under perfect calibration, from which we derive the risk probability $P_{\mathrm{risk}}$ that quantifies the statistical evidence for overconfidence. We further argue that overconfidence risk assessment must be complemented by a measure of discriminative value: whether the assigned confidences actively distinguish correct from incorrect predictions. We show that confidence-weighted accuracy $\mathrm{cwA}$ is the natural such complement, and that confidence-weighting extends to all standard classification metrics. In particular, we prove that the confidence-weighted AUC (cwAUC) captures the information about calibration while the classical AUC cannot. We validate the proposed indicators on several synthetic confidence distributions under multiple controlled calibration profiles and on fifteen real datasets with and without post-hoc calibration. Experiments demonstrate that CSR achieves near-perfect sensitivity and specificity across all tested conditions.

中文摘要翻译: 置信度校准的评估一直由期望校准误差（ECE）主导，这是一种线性度量，无论置信度处于何种水平，同等对待校准偏移。我们发现，即使在任意大的过度自信风险下，ECE仍可能保持很小的值，因此我们提出了校准尺寸比（CSR）作为替代，这是一个可解释的度量，在完美校准下取值为1，并由此导出了风险概率$P_{\mathrm{risk}}$，用于量化过度自信的统计证据。我们进一步论证，过度自信风险评估必须辅以判别能力的度量：即所分配的置信度能否有效区分正确与错误的预测。我们证明置信度加权准确率$\mathrm{cwA}$是这种自然的补充指标，且置信度加权可以扩展到所有标准分类指标。特别地，我们证明置信度加权的AUC（cwAUC）能够捕获校准信息，而经典AUC则不能。我们在多种受控校准曲线下的合成置信度分布上，以及在有无事后校准的十五个真实数据集上，验证了所提出的指标。实验表明，CSR在所有测试条件下均实现了接近完美的敏感性和特异性。

### [182] [Federated Semi-Supervised Graph Neural Networks with Prototype-Guided Pseudo-Labeling for Privacy-Preserving Gestational Diabetes Mellitus Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01810)
*G. Victor Daniela,A. Mallikarjuna Reddya,Uday Kumar Addankia,Sridhar Reddy Gogua,Sravanth Kumar Ramakuria*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出FedTGNN-SS，一种联邦半监督框架，通过k-NN图、原型伪标签、自适应图精炼和隐私保护的原型共享，在标签稀缺和数据隐私约束下实现GDM风险早期分层。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 真实临床部署机器学习面临标签稀缺（大量电子健康记录缺乏诊断标签）和数据隐私（无法跨医院共享患者级数据）两个耦合约束，现有方法难以同时解决这两个问题。

Method: (1) 每个医院构建局部k-NN患者相似图并训练拓扑自适应GNN编码器；(2) 原型引导的伪标签与邻域一致性；(3) 自适应图精炼，利用学习到的嵌入周期更新k-NN图；(4) 仅对连续变量施加临床感知的一致性增强；(5) 仅交换类级质心的隐私安全原型共享。

Result: 在三个糖尿病数据集（GDM: N=3,525; Pima: N=768; Early Stage: N=520）上，每站点10%-80%标签缺失条件下，FedTGNN-SS在11个联邦基线中取得56次显著胜出（p<0.05），极端稀缺下AUROC优异（Pima: 0.8037@80%缺失, Early Stage: 0.9634@80%缺失）。

Conclusion: FedTGNN-SS有效解决了标签稀缺与数据隐私的双重约束，在GDM早期风险分层中显著优于现有联邦方法。

Original Abstract: Gestational Diabetes Mellitus (GDM) is a high-prevalence pregnancy complication that requires accurate early risk stratification to reduce maternal and fetal morbidity. However, real-world clinical deployment of machine learning is hindered by two coupled constraints: (i) label scarcity, where a large fraction of electronic health records (EHR) lack confirmed diagnostic labels, and (ii) data privacy, which prevents sharing patient-level data across hospitals. This paper proposes FedTGNN-SS, a privacy-preserving federated semi-supervised framework for clinical tabular EHR. Each hospital builds a local k-nearest-neighbor patient similarity graph and trains a topology-adaptive GNN encoder. To robustly exploit unlabeled records, FedTGNN-SS combines (1) prototype-guided pseudo-labeling with neighborhood agreement, (2) adaptive graph refinement that periodically updates the k-NN graph using learned embeddings, (3) clinical-aware consistency augmentation applied only to continuous variables, and (4) privacy-safe prototype sharing that exchanges only class-level centroids. Across three diabetes-related datasets (GDM: N = 3,525; Pima: N = 768; Early Stage: N = 520) under 10\%-80\% missing labels per silo, FedTGNN-SS achieves 56 significant wins ($p < 0.05$) against 11 federated baselines and attains strong AUROC under extreme scarcity (Pima: 0.8037 at 80\% missing, Early Stage: 0.9634 at 80\% missing).

中文摘要翻译: 妊娠期糖尿病（GDM）是一种高发病率的妊娠并发症，需要准确的早期风险分层以降低母婴发病率。然而，机器学习在真实临床部署中面临两个耦合约束：（i）标签稀缺，即大量电子健康记录（EHR）缺乏确诊的诊断标签；（ii）数据隐私，即无法跨医院共享患者级数据。本文提出FedTGNN-SS，一种面向临床表格型EHR的隐私保护联邦半监督框架。每个医院构建局部k-近邻患者相似图并训练拓扑自适应GNN编码器。为稳健地利用未标注记录，FedTGNN-SS结合了（1）带有邻域一致性的原型引导伪标签，（2）利用学习到的嵌入定期更新k-NN图的自适应图精炼，（3）仅作用于连续变量的临床感知一致性增强，以及（4）仅交换类别级质心的隐私安全原型共享。在三个糖尿病相关数据集（GDM: N=3,525; Pima: N=768; Early Stage: N=520）上，每站点标签缺失率为10%-80%的条件下，FedTGNN-SS在11个联邦基线方法中取得56次显著胜出（p<0.05），并在极端标签稀缺下达到强劲的AUROC（Pima: 0.8037 at 80%缺失, Early Stage: 0.9634 at 80%缺失）。

</details>


### [183] [Skipping the Zeros in Diffusion Models for Sparse Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01817)
*Phil Sidney Ostheimer,Mayank Nagda,Andriy Balinskyy,Gabriel Vicente Rodrigues,Jean Radig,Carl Herrmann,Stephan Mandt,Marius Kloft,Sophie Fellenz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Sparsity-Exploiting Diffusion (SED)，一种专为稀疏连续数据设计的扩散模型，通过仅对非零值建模来保留稀疏性，在训练和推理时跳过零值，从而在保持或提升生成质量的同时节省计算量。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 传统扩散模型擅长处理稠密连续数据，但无法有效处理稀疏连续数据——它们会抹除稀疏模式，对大量零值进行不必要的计算，且无法建模代表信号有意缺失的精确零值。

Method: SED仅对非零值进行建模，在训练和推理阶段跳过零值计算，从而保留数据的稀疏结构。

Result: 在物理和生物基准测试中，SED匹配或超越了传统扩散模型及领域特定基线；视觉实验直观展示了稠密扩散模型的局限性以及SED的优势。

Conclusion: SED能够在保持或提升生成质量的前提下实现计算量的节省，为稀疏连续数据的生成建模提供了一种有效的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Diffusion models (DMs) excel on dense continuous data, but are not designed for sparse continuous data. They do not model exact zeros that represent the deliberate absence of a signal. As a result, they erase sparsity patterns and perform unnecessary computation on mostly zero entries. With Sparsity-Exploiting Diffusion (SED), we model only non-zero values, preserving sparsity. SED delivers computational savings while maintaining or improving generation quality by skipping zeros during training and inference. Across physics and biology benchmarks, SED matches or surpasses conventional DMs and domain-specific baselines, while vision experiments provide intuitive insights into the limitations of dense DMs and the benefits of SED.

中文摘要翻译: 扩散模型（DMs）在稠密连续数据上表现出色，但并非为稀疏连续数据设计。它们无法建模代表信号有意缺失的精确零值，因此会抹除稀疏模式，并对大量零值条目执行不必要的计算。本文提出稀疏性利用扩散模型（Sparsity-Exploiting Diffusion, SED），仅对非零值进行建模，从而保留稀疏性。SED在训练和推理过程中跳过零值，在保持或提升生成质量的同时实现计算量的节省。在物理和生物基准测试中，SED匹配甚至超越了传统扩散模型及领域特定基线，而视觉实验则为稠密扩散模型的局限性以及SED的优势提供了直观的理解。

### [184] [Selector-Guided Autonomous Curriculum for One-Shot Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01823)
*Rudray Dave,Vedang Dubey,Smit Deoghare,Sudhakar Mishra*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于可学习选择器的自主课程学习（SGAC）方法，通过多维特征空间（包括成功概率、奖励方差、输出分歧（熵）和语义难度）替代静态奖励方差启发式，在1-shot GRPO训练中动态筛选高质量问题实例，在MATH基准上以Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B模型达到68.0%的准确率，优于SOTA方法的64.0%和Wang等人的66.0%。核心发现是输出分歧（熵）比奖励方差更能预测推理增益。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）模型在1-shot场景下依赖基于历史奖励方差的启发式方法选择实例，但这种静态启发式在衡量实例的可迁移价值上存在根本性误导，亟需更有效的实例选择策略来提升推理能力。

Method: 提出选择器引导的自主课程学习（SGAC）方法：设计一个可学习的选择器模型，在包含成功概率、奖励方差、输出分歧（熵）和语义难度水平的多维特征空间上对候选问题进行排序，动态地从大规模问题池中筛选高质量实例，并以微批次方式执行1-shot GRPO训练，实现自主课程学习。

Result: 在Hendrycks MATH基准上，以Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B为基线，SGAC方法在留出集上达到68.0%的准确率，优于SOTA模型的64.0%和Wang等人1-shot RLVR检查点的66.0%。实验发现输出分歧（熵）是比奖励方差更强的推理增益预测指标。

Conclusion: 基于熵的智能数据筛选能够在严格有限数据条件下相对于静态训练方法带来严格的推理能力提升，输出分歧是衡量实例可迁移价值的关键指标。

Original Abstract: Recently, Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has been established as a highly effective technique for augmenting the math reasoning skills of Large Language Models (LLMs) based on a single instance. Current state-of-the-art 1-shot RLVR models adopt heuristics for selecting instances, mostly based on historical variance in rewards, which we find to be inherently misleading as a measure of transferability value. In this paper, we propose a Selector-Guided Autonomous Curriculum (SGAC) approach, which employs a learnable selector model on a multi-dimensional feature space consisting of success probability, reward variance, output disagreement (entropy), and semantic difficulty level, instead of the static reward variance heuristic. In our empirical evaluation on pools of candidate problems, we observed that output disagreement, rather than reward variance, is the strongest predictor of reasoning gains in subsequent iterations. Leveraging this finding, we develop an autonomous curriculum algorithm for dynamically siphoning candidate problems from a large pool, ranking them by the learned selector, and running micro-bursts of 1-shot GRPO. Our framework is evaluated using the Hendrycks MATH benchmark, with the Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B model serving as the baseline. Our framework obtains an accuracy of 68.0\% on the hold-out dataset, which is better than the accuracy obtained from the state-of-the-art model, 64.0\%, as well as the 1-shot RLVR checkpoint proposed by Wang et al., which achieved an accuracy of 66.0\%. The results confirm that entropy-based intelligent data curation leads to strict reasoning improvement over static training methods, particularly in severely limited data conditions.

中文摘要翻译: 最近，基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已被确认为一种基于单个实例增强大型语言模型（LLMs）数学推理能力的高效技术。当前最先进的1-shot RLVR模型采用基于历史奖励方差的启发式方法选择实例，但我们发现这种方法在衡量可迁移价值方面存在根本性误导。本文提出了一种选择器引导的自主课程学习（SGAC）方法，该方法采用一个可学习的选择器模型，在由成功概率、奖励方差、输出分歧（熵）和语义难度水平构成的多维特征空间上进行选择，而非使用静态的奖励方差启发式。在候选问题池上的实证评估中，我们观察到输出分歧（而非奖励方差）是后续迭代中推理增益的最强预测指标。基于这一发现，我们开发了一种自主课程学习算法，用于从大规模问题池中动态筛选候选问题，通过习得的选择器进行排序，并执行微批次的1-shot GRPO训练。我们使用Hendrycks MATH基准对框架进行评估，以Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B模型作为基线。我们的框架在留出数据集上获得了68.0%的准确率，优于当前最先进模型获得的64.0%准确率，以及Wang等人提出的1-shot RLVR检查点所达到的66.0%准确率。结果证实，基于熵的智能数据筛选能够在严格有限的数据条件下，相对于静态训练方法带来严格的推理能力提升。

### [185] [Learning Koopman operators for coupled systems via information on governing equations of subsystems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01835)
*Tatsuya Naoi,Jun Ohkubo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对耦合系统中EDMD在数据有限时不稳定、不准确的问题，提出利用子系统微分方程学习Koopman算子的方法，并在耦合振荡器系统中验证了有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 非线性耦合系统维度高、子系统交互复杂，现有基于Koopman算子的EDMD方法纯数据驱动，在数据有限时对耦合系统不稳定且不准确。

Method: 利用每个子系统的微分方程来学习耦合系统的Koopman算子，将物理先验知识融入算子学习过程。

Result: 在耦合振荡器系统上的数值实验验证了所提方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 结合子系统微分方程先验知识的方法能够更稳定、准确地学习耦合系统的Koopman算子，优于纯数据驱动的EDMD。

Original Abstract: Nonlinear coupled systems are ubiquitous in science and engineering. The analysis and modeling of such systems is challenging due to their high dimensionality and complex interactions among subsystems. In recent years, operator-theoretic methods based on the Koopman operator have attracted attention as a powerful tool for analyzing and modeling nonlinear dynamical systems. Extended dynamic mode decomposition (EDMD) is one of the most popular methods to approximate the Koopman operator. However, EDMD is a purely data-driven method, and it could be unstable and inaccurate for coupled systems under limited data availability. In this paper, we propose a method to learn the Koopman operator for coupled systems using the differential equations governing each subsystem. We also demonstrate its effectiveness through numerical experiments on coupled oscillator systems.

中文摘要翻译: 非线性耦合系统在科学和工程中无处不在。由于系统的高维性和子系统间的复杂交互，对此类系统的分析与建模具有挑战性。近年来，基于Koopman算子的算子理论学习方法作为分析和建模非线性动力系统的有力工具而受到关注。扩展动态模式分解（EDMD）是逼近Koopman算子的最流行方法之一。然而，EDMD是一种纯数据驱动的方法，在数据有限的情况下，它对耦合系统的估计可能不稳定且不准确。本文提出了一种利用每个子系统的微分方程来学习耦合系统Koopman算子的方法。我们通过在耦合振荡器系统上的数值实验验证了其有效性。

### [186] [QHyer: Q-conditioned Hybrid Attention-mamba Transformer for Offline Goal-conditioned RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01862)
*Xing Lei,Jincheng Wang,Xuetao Zhang,Donglin Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对离线目标条件强化学习（GCRL）中数据集部分可观测、依赖长度异质以及稀疏奖励下RTG缺乏区分度的问题，提出QHyer，用流参数化的Q估计器替代RTG以支持跨演示拼接，并引入门控混合注意力-Mamba主干实现内容自适应历史压缩，在非马尔可夫和马尔可夫数据集上达到SOTA。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 离线GCRL的现实数据集常呈现部分可观测性和历史依赖性，混合了马尔可夫与非马尔可夫特性，违反标准RL假设。现有方法中，纯Transformer处理长程上下文时效率低且对局部马尔可夫结构处理脆弱；混合架构（如LSDT）使用固定窗口提取器无法自适应不同长度的依赖关系，常截断长程上下文。此外，稀疏奖励下RTG在子轨迹间缺乏区分度，无法有效指导目标达成行为的拼接。

Method: 提出QHyer框架：(1) 用流参数化、状态条件的Q估计器替代RTG，提供跨演示拼接信号；(2) 设计门控混合注意力-Mamba主干，结合注意力的局部建模能力与Mamba的状态空间模型长程压缩能力，实现内容自适应历史压缩，同时保留局部动态。

Result: 在非马尔可夫和马尔可夫数据集上均达到SOTA性能，验证了模型在多样化场景下的有效性。

Conclusion: QHyer通过替代RTG的Q估计器与混合注意力-Mamba架构，有效解决了离线GCRL中依赖长度异质和稀疏奖励下信号不足的问题，为异构时序依赖建模提供了新范式。

Original Abstract: Offline goal-conditioned RL (GCRL) learns goal-reaching policies from static datasets, but real-world datasets are often partially observable and history-dependent, exhibiting a mix of Markovian and non-Markovian that violate standard RL assumptions. History-aware sequence models such as Decision Transformer (DT) are a natural fit for long-term dependency modeling, yet pure attention is inefficient and brittle when handling local Markovian structure and long-range context simultaneously. Although recent hybrid architectures (e.g., LSDT) introduce local extractors to improve local dependencies modeling, the fixed-window extraction cannot adapt its effective memory to varying dependency lengths in temporally heterogeneous settings, often truncating long-range context rather than compressing its content adaptively. Moreover, sequential offline GCRL faces a key bottleneck: under sparse rewards, return-to-go (RTG) becomes non-discriminative across sub-trajectories, providing little guidance signal for stitching goal-reaching behaviors from diverse demonstrations. To address these, we propose \textbf{QHyer}, which replaces RTG with a flow-parameterized, state-conditioned goal-reaching Q-estimator to support stitching across demonstrations, and introduces a gated Hybrid Attention-Mamba backbone that performs content-adaptive history compression while preserving local dynamics. Extensive experiments demonstrate that \textbf{QHyer} achieves state-of-the-art performance on both non-Markovian and Markovian datasets, validating its effectiveness for diverse scenarios.

中文摘要翻译: 离线目标条件强化学习（GCRL）从静态数据集中学习目标达成策略，但现实世界的数据集通常是部分可观测且历史依赖的，表现出马尔可夫性和非马尔可夫性的混合特征，违反标准强化学习假设。历史感知序列模型（如决策Transformer）天然适合长程依赖建模，但纯注意力机制在处理局部马尔可夫结构和长程上下文时效率低下且脆弱。尽管最近的混合架构（如LSDT）引入了局部提取器来改善局部依赖建模，但固定窗口提取无法自适应调整其有效记忆长度以应对时序异质场景中变化的依赖长度，常常截断长程上下文而非自适应地压缩其内容。此外，序列化离线GCRL面临一个关键瓶颈：在稀疏奖励下，返回目标（RTG）在子轨迹间变得非区分性，无法为从多样演示中拼接目标达成行为提供有效的指导信号。为解决这些问题，我们提出\textbf{QHyer}，该方法用流参数化、状态条件的目标达成Q估计器替代RTG以支持跨演示拼接，并引入门控混合注意力-Mamba主干，在保留局部动态的同时实现内容自适应历史压缩。大量实验表明，\textbf{QHyer}在非马尔可夫和马尔可夫数据集上均达到了最先进性能，验证了其在多样化场景中的有效性。

### [187] [Robust Conditional Conformal Prediction via Branched Normalizing Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01868)
*Rui Xu,Xingyuan Chen,Wenxing Huang,Minxuan Huang,Weiyan Chen,Sihong Xie,Hui Xiong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了分布偏移下保形预测的条件覆盖有效性问题，提出了基于Wasserstein距离的理论边界，并设计了分支归一化流（BNF）架构来缓解条件覆盖退化，在九个数据集上验证了其有效性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有保形预测方法在分布偏移下仅能保证边际覆盖，无法控制单个测试输入的条件覆盖误差，导致模型在条件分数分布不匹配的区域不可靠。亟需一种能同时保证条件覆盖鲁棒性的方法。

Method: 首先从理论上用Wasserstein距离刻画了分布偏移下条件覆盖无效性的边界，揭示了可逆传输在缓解条件覆盖退化中的关键作用。基于此洞察，提出了分支归一化流（BNF）——一种双分支架构：一个分支将测试输入归一化到校准分布，另一个分支将归一化输入的预测集变换回测试分布，从而保持条件覆盖保证。

Result: 在九个数据集上，BNF在广泛的置信水平下持续提升了条件覆盖的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 可逆传输能够有效缓解分布偏移下保形预测的条件覆盖退化问题，BNF架构是一种实用的解决方案。

Original Abstract: Conformal prediction (CP) constructs prediction sets with marginal coverage guarantees under the assumption that the calibration and test distributions are identical. However, under distribution shift, existing approaches primarily align marginal conformal score distributions, which is sufficient to preserve marginal coverage but does not control the conditional coverage error at individual test inputs. As a consequence, CP can remain unreliable in regions where the conditional score distributions are mismatched. In this work, we bound the conditional invalidity of CP under distribution shift in terms of the Wasserstein distance between the calibration and test distributions. This result highlights the role of invertible transport in mitigating conditional coverage degradation. Motivated by this insight, we introduce Branched Normalizing Flow (BNF), a two-branch architecture that normalizes a test input to the calibration distribution and transforms the prediction set of the normalized input back to the test distribution while preserving conditional guarantees. Empirically, BNF consistently improves conditional coverage robustness on nine datasets across a wide range of confidence levels.

中文摘要翻译: 保形预测（CP）在校准分布与测试分布相同的假设下构建具有边际覆盖保证的预测集。然而，在分布偏移下，现有方法主要对齐边际保形分数分布，这足以保持边际覆盖，但无法控制单个测试输入的条件覆盖误差。因此，CP在条件分数分布不匹配的区域仍然不可靠。本文在Wasserstein距离的框架下，刻画了分布偏移下CP条件无效性的边界。该结果凸显了可逆传输在缓解条件覆盖退化中的关键作用。受此启发，我们提出了分支归一化流（BNF）——一种双分支架构，它将测试输入归一化到校准分布，并将归一化输入的预测集变换回测试分布，同时保持条件覆盖保证。实验结果表明，在九个数据集上、广泛的置信水平下，BNF持续提升了条件覆盖的鲁棒性。

</details>


### [188] [Leveraging Data Symmetries to Select an Optimal Subset of Training Data under Label Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01874)
*Kumar Shubham,Pavan Karjol,Kiran M K,Prathosh AP*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从理论上证明了基于cutstats方法在含噪数据集中选择子集训练分类器的性能受k-NN精度影响，并指出在高维噪声环境下，利用数据不变性和对称性知识可以显著提升k-NN性能，使其接近贝叶斯最优分类器；对于真实场景中不变性知识部分已知的情况，学习不变表示仍有助于识别近似最优子集。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有方法cutstats通过k-NN检测低噪声样本以在含噪数据集中选择子集，但其在高维数据上的性能尚未被充分探索，本文旨在从理论上分析并改进该方法在高维噪声环境下的表现。

Method: 形式化建立了cutstats所选子集训练的分类器性能与k-NN精度之间的理论联系；提出利用数据不变性和对称性知识增强k-NN在高维噪声环境下的性能；对于不变性知识部分未知的真实场景，采用学习不变表示的方法来识别近似最优子集。

Result: 理论证明表明cutstats子集分类器性能受k-NN精度影响；在噪声环境下，利用数据不变性和对称性知识可显著提升k-NN性能，使其在高维下接近贝叶斯最优分类器；当不变性知识部分已知时，学习的不变表示仍有助于识别近似最优子集。

Conclusion: 利用数据不变性和对称性知识能有效提升cutstats在高维噪声数据上的子集选择性能，且即使仅部分已知不变性知识，通过学习不变表示也能取得近似最优结果。

Original Abstract: The performance of machine learning models often relies on large labeled datasets; however, data collected from diverse sources can contain label noise. Recent work has shown that, in noisy settings, there may exist a subset of the training data on which models can achieve performance comparable to training on a noise-free dataset. A widely used method for identifying such subsets is cutstats, which employs k-nearest neighbors (k-NN) to detect low-noise samples. However, its performance on high-dimensional data remains largely unexplored. In this work, we formally establish that the performance of a classifier trained on a subset of a noisy dataset selected via cutstats is influenced by the accuracy of k-NN. We further demonstrate that, in noisy environments, exploiting data invariance and knowledge of underlying symmetries can significantly enhance the performance of k-NN, bringing it closer to the Bayes optimal classifier even in high-dimensional regimes. Finally, we show that for real-world scenarios, where information about the underlying invariance is only partially known, learnt invariant representations can still facilitate the identification of near-optimal subsets.

中文摘要翻译: 机器学习模型的性能通常依赖于大规模标注数据集；然而，从不同来源收集的数据可能包含标签噪声。近期研究表明，在噪声环境下，训练数据中可能存在一个子集，使得模型在其上训练能达到与在无噪声数据集上训练相当的性能。识别此类子集的一种广泛使用的方法是cutstats，它采用k近邻（k-NN）来检测低噪声样本。然而，cutstats在高维数据上的性能尚未得到充分探索。在本工作中，我们形式化地证明了：基于cutstats从含噪数据集中选择子集训练的分类器性能受k-NN精度的影响。我们进一步证明，在噪声环境下，利用数据不变性和底层对称性知识可以显著提升k-NN的性能，使其在高维场景下也能接近贝叶斯最优分类器。最后，我们表明，对于真实世界中底层不变性知识仅部分已知的场景，学习得到的不变表示仍然有助于识别近似最优的子集。

### [189] [How Label Imbalance Shapes Geometry: A General Spectral Analysis of Multi-Label Neural Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01897)
*Xiaoxuan Ma,Yixuan Yang,Song Li,Xiangyun Hui*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文将神经坍缩（Neural Collapse）从多分类推广到多标签分类，提出谱控制框架，揭示了标签协方差谱控制终态几何结构，并解决了多重性不平衡猜想。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 现有研究假设标签平衡和组合对称性，忽略了多标签分类中标签相关性和数据不平衡导致的几何失真，缺乏对不平衡多标签场景下神经坍缩的理论理解。

Method: 提出谱控制框架（spectral-control framework），引入标签协方差谱 κ_m 作为控制分布相关下界几何的标量，通过分析标签分布的二阶矩矩阵来刻画终端阶段几何的稳定性。

Result: 证明经典标签平均结构仅在完美正交条件下成立；高多重性原型遵循类频率加权合成规则而非均匀平均；标签协方差谱量化了最弱中心化类间对比方向，控制终端几何稳定性。

Conclusion: 解决了不平衡猜想中的缩放平均问题，建立了将神经坍缩扩展到复杂不平衡多标签环境的统一理论框架。

Original Abstract: This work investigates the phenomenon of Neural Collapse (NC) in multi-label classification, extending its conceptual framework from multi-class learning to general correlated and imbalanced multi-label settings. Although recent studies have identified a ''tag-wise averaging'' structure for multi-label features, this view relies on implicit assumptions of label balance and combinatorial symmetry. Consequently, it fails to account for the geometrical distortions caused by intrinsic label correlations and data imbalance, which are common in practice. We resolve the multiplicity-one imbalance conjecture raised by Li et al. (2024), showing that higher-multiplicity prototypes obey a class-frequency-weighted synthesis rule rather than uniform averaging. To address this, we propose a rigorous spectral-control framework to analyze the terminal phase of multi-label learning under general imbalanced conditions. We introduce the label covariance spectrum $κ_m$, a scalar controlling the distribution-dependent lower-bound geometry, derived from the second-order moment matrix of the label distribution. Contrary to the averaging perspective, our analysis reveals that the centered label covariance spectrum controls the stability of terminal geometry by quantifying the weakest centered inter-class contrast directions. We prove that the classical Tag-wise Averaging emerges only as a special case under perfect orthogonality. Numerical experiments on synthetic distributions validate our theoretical bounds. This work resolves the scaled-average aspect of the imbalance conjecture and establishes a unifying theoretical framework that extends Neural Collapse to complex, imbalanced multi-label settings.

中文摘要翻译: 本研究探讨了多标签分类中的神经坍缩（Neural Collapse, NC）现象，将其概念框架从多类学习推广到一般相关且不平衡的多标签设置。尽管近期研究发现多标签特征存在"标签平均"结构，但该观点依赖于标签平衡和组合对称性的隐含假设，因此无法解释由内在标签相关性和数据不平衡引起的几何失真——而这些问题在实践中普遍存在。我们解决了Li等人（2024）提出的多重性不平衡猜想，证明高多重性原型服从类频率加权合成规则，而非均匀平均。为此，我们提出了一个严格的谱控制框架，用于分析一般不平衡条件下多标签学习的终端阶段。我们引入标签协方差谱 κ_m，该标量由标签分布的二阶矩矩阵导出，用于控制依赖于分布的下界几何。与平均化视角相反，我们的分析揭示：中心化标签协方差谱通过量化最弱的中心化类间对比方向，从而控制终端几何的稳定性。我们证明，经典的标签平均结构仅在完美正交条件下作为特例出现。在合成分布上的数值实验验证了我们的理论界。这项工作解决了不平衡猜想中的缩放平均问题，并建立了一个统一的理论框架，将神经坍缩推广到复杂、不平衡的多标签设置。

</details>


### [190] [Stochastic Sparse Attention for Memory-Bound Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01910)
*Kyle Lee,Corentin Delacour,Kevin Callahan-Coray,Kyle Jiang,Can Yaras,Samet Oymak,Tathagata Srimani,Kerem Y. Camsari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SANTA通过随机稀疏化注意力机制中的值访问和得分计算，实现无乘法的高效自回归解码，在长上下文场景下获得1.5倍注意力核加速。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 自回归解码在长上下文场景下受限于带宽瓶颈，因为生成每个token都需要从KV缓存中读取所有键值向量，导致计算效率低下。

Method: 提出随机加性无乘法注意力（SANTA），通过从后softmax分布中采样少量索引来稀疏化值缓存访问，并用gather-and-add替代值阶段的多乘累加。同时提出分层抽样降低方差，以及伯努利qK^T采样进一步稀疏化得分阶段。

Result: 在NVIDIA RTX 6000 Ada上，相比FlashInfer和FlashDecoding实现1.5倍解码步注意力核加速，在32k token上下文中保持基线精度。

Conclusion: SANTA与三元量化、低秩投影、KV缓存压缩等上游技术正交，共同指向稀疏、无乘法和能效高的推理方法。

Original Abstract: Autoregressive decoding becomes bandwidth-limited at long contexts, as generating each token requires reading all $n_k$ key and value vectors from KV cache. We present Stochastic Additive No-mulT Attention (SANTA), a method that sparsifies value-cache access by sampling $S \ll n_k$ indices from the post-softmax distribution and aggregates only those value rows. This yields an unbiased estimator of the post-softmax value aggregation while replacing value-stage multiply-accumulates with gather-and-add. We introduce stratified sampling to design variance-reduced, GPU-friendly variants, demonstrating $1.5\times$ decode-step attention kernel speedup over FlashInfer and FlashDecoding on an NVIDIA RTX 6000 Ada while matching baseline accuracy at 32k-token contexts. Finally, we propose Bernoulli $qK^\mathsf{T}$ sampling as a complementary technique to sparsify the score stage, reducing key-feature access through stochastic ternary queries. Both methods are orthogonal to upstream techniques such as ternary quantization, low-rank projections, and KV-cache compression. Together, they point toward sparse, multiplier-free, and energy-efficient inference. We open-source our kernels at: https://github.com/OPUSLab/SANTA.git

中文摘要翻译: 自回归解码在长上下文场景下受限于带宽瓶颈，因为生成每个token需要从KV缓存中读取所有$n_k$个键（Key）和值（Value）向量。我们提出随机加性无乘法注意力（Stochastic Additive No-mulT Attention, SANTA），该方法通过从后softmax分布中采样$S \ll n_k$个索引来稀疏化值缓存访问，并仅聚合这些值行。这产生了一个后softmax值聚合的无偏估计器，同时将值阶段的多乘累加（multiply-accumulates）替换为聚集加操作（gather-and-add）。我们引入分层抽样来设计方差缩减且GPU友好的变体，在NVIDIA RTX 6000 Ada上相比FlashInfer和FlashDecoding实现了1.5倍的解码步注意力核加速，同时在32k token上下文中匹配基线精度。最后，我们提出伯努利$qK^\mathsf{T}$采样作为得分阶段稀疏化的互补技术，通过随机三元查询减少特征访问。这两种方法与三元量化、低秩投影和KV缓存压缩等上游技术正交。它们共同指向稀疏、无乘法和能效高的推理方法。我们已在https://github.com/OPUSLab/SANTA.git开源了相关内核。

</details>


### [191] [RefusalGuard: Geometry-Preserving Fine-Tuning for Safety in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01913)
*Sadia Asif,Mohammad Mohammadi Amiri*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了标准微调会导致安全相关表征发生系统性漂移、几何结构扭曲以及任务优化与安全特征之间的干扰，从而破坏对齐安全性；为此提出了REFUSALGUARD，一种在表征空间层面约束更新的微调框架，能够在保持安全中介组件稳定的同时允许任务学习，在多个模型家族和对抗安全基准上实现了接近原始安全对齐模型的攻击成功率，同时保持竞争性的任务性能。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 先前工作表明安全相关特征编码在模型激活空间的结构化表征中，但微调过程中这些表征如何变化以及对齐为何退化的问题尚未得到充分理解。

Method: REFUSALGUARD是一种表征级微调框架，通过约束隐藏表征空间中的更新来保持安全相关结构，确保安全中介组件在模型适配过程中保持稳定，同时允许在互补方向上进行任务特定学习。

Result: 在LLaMA、Gemma和Qwen等多个模型家族上，使用AdvBench、DirectHarm4和JailbreakBench等对抗安全基准评估，REFUSALGUARD实现了与原始安全对齐模型相当的攻击成功率，同时保持了竞争性的下游任务性能，显著优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 标准微调会系统性地破坏安全相关表征的结构导致对齐退化，而REFUSALGUARD通过表征层面的约束有效缓解了这一问题，为安全微调提供了新的范式。

Original Abstract: Fine-tuning safety-aligned language models for downstream tasks often leads to substantial degradation of refusal behavior, making models vulnerable to adversarial misuse. While prior work has shown that safety-relevant features are encoded in structured representations within the model's activation space, how these representations change during fine-tuning and why alignment degrades remains poorly understood. In this work, we investigate the representation-level mechanisms underlying alignment degradation. Our analysis shows that standard fine-tuning induces systematic drift in safety-relevant representations, distorts their geometric structure, and introduces interference between task optimization and safety features. These effects collectively lead to increased harmful compliance. Motivated by these findings, we introduce REFUSALGUARD, a representation-level fine-tuning framework that preserves safety-relevant structure during model adaptation. Our approach constrains updates in hidden representation space, ensuring that safety-mediating components remain stable while allowing task-specific learning in complementary directions. We evaluate REFUSALGUARD across multiple model families, including LLaMA, Gemma, and Qwen, on adversarial safety benchmarks such as AdvBench, DirectHarm4, and JailbreakBench, as well as downstream utility tasks. Our approach achieves attack success rates comparable to base safety-aligned models while maintaining competitive task performance, significantly outperforming baselines.

中文摘要翻译: 将安全对齐的语言模型微调至下游任务通常会导致拒绝行为的显著退化，使模型容易受到对抗性滥用。虽然先前的工作表明安全相关特征编码在模型激活空间中的结构化表征中，但这些表征在微调过程中如何变化以及对齐为何退化仍未被充分理解。在本工作中，我们研究了对齐退化背后的表征级机制。我们的分析表明，标准微调会导致安全相关表征发生系统性漂移，扭曲其几何结构，并引入任务优化与安全特征之间的干扰。这些效应共同导致了有害遵从性的增加。受这些发现启发，我们引入了REFUSALGUARD，一种表征级的微调框架，在模型适配过程中保持安全相关结构。我们的方法约束隐藏表征空间中的更新，确保安全中介组件保持稳定，同时允许在互补方向上进行任务特定学习。我们在多个模型家族（包括LLaMA、Gemma和Qwen）上，使用AdvBench、DirectHarm4和JailbreakBench等对抗安全基准以及下游实用性任务对REFUSALGUARD进行了评估。我们的方法实现了与基础安全对齐模型相当的攻击成功率，同时保持了竞争性的任务性能，显著优于基线方法。

### [192] [Pandora's Regret: A Proper Scoring Rule for Evaluating Sequential Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01936)
*Gerardo A. Flores,Yash Deshpande,Jannis R. Brea,Ashia C. Wilson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Pandora's Regret，一种适用于顺序搜索场景的成对可加严格恰当评分规则，解决了标准评分规则（如对数损失）与搜索效用不对齐的问题，并在MedMNIST模型上验证了其优越性。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 标准严格恰当评分规则（如对数损失）是局部的，忽略了候选项的排序信息，与顺序搜索场景下的实际效用不一致，因此需要一种与搜索效用对齐的评分规则。

Method: 通过分析可变测试成本下最优搜索的期望成本，推导出Pandora's Regret——一种闭式、成对可加、严格恰当的评分规则；进一步构建了单参数Beta族，在排序交换惩罚与概率幅度之间取得平衡。

Result: 在597个MedMNIST模型上的实验表明，基于Pandora的指标比标准替代指标（如对数损失、准确率、宏F1）能更好地预测临床诊断成本；同时证明对数损失、准确率和宏F1依赖于与顺序搜索不一致的隐式决策模型。

Conclusion: Pandora's Regret将决策理论驱动的评分规则构建扩展到多分类设置，为顺序搜索任务提供了与效用对齐的评估指标。

Original Abstract: In sequential search, alternatives are tested until the true class is found. Standard proper scoring rules like log loss are local, ignoring the ranking of competitors and misaligning model evaluation with search utility. We show that sequential search induces a pairwise structure that overcomes this. By analyzing the expected cost of optimal search under varying testing costs, we derive Pandora's Regret: a closed-form, pairwise-additive, and strictly proper scoring rule. Pandora's Regret both elicits true probabilities and penalizes rank-reversing miscalibrations where distractors outrank the true class. Our construction yields a one-parameter Beta family that balances penalties for rank-swapping versus probability magnitude, while retaining a grounded interpretation as expected search cost. We prove that log loss, accuracy, and macro-F1 rely on implicit decision models misaligned with sequential search. Across 597 MedMNIST models, Pandora-based metrics better predict clinical diagnostic costs than standard alternatives, extending decision-theoretic scoring rule construction to the multiclass setting.

中文摘要翻译: 在顺序搜索中，备选项被逐一测试直到找到真实类别。标准的严格恰当评分规则（如对数损失）具有局部性，忽略了候选项的排序信息，导致模型评估与搜索效用不一致。本文表明，顺序搜索具有一种能克服这一缺陷的成对结构。通过分析可变测试成本下最优搜索的期望成本，我们推导出Pandora's Regret：一个闭式、成对可加且严格恰当的评分规则。Pandora's Regret既能 elicit 真实概率，又能惩罚干扰项排名超过真实类别的排序反转式误校准。我们的构造产生了一个单参数Beta族，在排序交换惩罚与概率幅度之间取得平衡，同时保持了作为期望搜索成本的基于解释。我们证明，对数损失、准确率和宏F1依赖于与顺序搜索不一致的隐式决策模型。在597个MedMNIST模型上，基于Pandora的指标比标准替代指标能更好地预测临床诊断成本，将决策理论驱动的评分规则构建扩展到多分类设置。

</details>

### [193] [Measuring Understanding Through Discrete Compositional Knowledge Structures in Hierarchical Automata](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01430)
*Igor Balaz*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出通过层次自动机架构将人工智能系统的理解能力转化为可测量的离散结构签名，解决当前概率系统、实践系统和神经系统中存在的“测量鸿沟”问题。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 当前人工智能系统对“理解”的测量存在空白：概率系统逐步调整置信度，基于实践的系统通过重复执行编译知识，神经系统将理解分散在 opaque 的嵌入空间中，缺乏对真实理解程度进行可量化评估的手段。

Method: 构建由有限状态机（表示模式）和高阶自动机（表示组合）组成的层次自动机架构。通过约束推理从单次观测构建自动机，利用相似性检测聚类相关自动机以量化概念鲁棒性，采用图记忆使组合知识可直接检视，并引入元认知机制实现可观测的重配置。

Result: 在简单几何域上的实验表明，图演化跟踪可揭示五种可测量的理解签名：即时表征形成、结构知识、泛化能力、组合意识和元认知访问。这些测量能够区分结构理解与统计相关性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个通过离散组合知识结构使理解变得可测量的框架，该测量能力可补充神经系统的感知学习和神经符号架构的任务执行。

Original Abstract: How do we measure genuine understanding in artificial cognitive systems? Current approaches face a measurement gap: probabilistic systems refine confidence gradually, practice-based systems compile knowledge through repeated execution, and neural systems distribute understanding across opaque embedding spaces. We propose that making understanding measurable requires architectures where understanding formation produces discrete, inspectable structural signatures. This paper presents hierarchical automata built from finite state machines representing patterns and higher-order automata representing compositions. Constrained inference constructs automata from single observations. Similarity detection clusters related automata, making concept robustness quantifiable. Graph memory makes compositional knowledge directly inspectable. Metacognitive mechanisms enable observable reconfiguration. We demonstrate understanding measurement in a simple geometric domain. Graph evolution tracking reveals five measurable signatures: immediate representation formation, structural knowledge, generalization capacity, compositional awareness, and metacognitive access. These measurements distinguish structural understanding from statistical correlation. Our contribution is a framework for making understanding measurable through discrete compositional knowledge structures. This measurement capability complements perceptual learning in neural systems and task execution in neurosymbolic architectures.

中文摘要翻译: 我们如何衡量人工认知系统中的真正理解？当前方法面临一个测量鸿沟：概率系统逐步调整置信度，基于实践的系统通过重复执行编译知识，神经系统则将理解分散在不透明的嵌入空间中。我们提出，要使理解变得可测量，需要构建这样一种架构——理解的形成会产生离散的、可检视的结构签名。本文提出了由表示模式的有限状态机和表示组合的高阶自动机构成的层次自动机。约束推理从单次观测中构建自动机。相似性检测聚类相关自动机，使概念鲁棒性变得可量化。图记忆使组合知识可直接检视。元认知机制实现可观测的重配置。我们在一个简单几何域上展示了理解测量。图演化跟踪揭示了五种可测量的签名：即时表征形成、结构知识、泛化能力、组合意识和元认知访问。这些测量能够区分结构理解与统计相关性。我们的贡献在于提出了一个通过离散组合知识结构使理解变得可测量的框架。该测量能力可补充神经系统的感知学习和神经符号架构中的任务执行。

</details>


### [194] [Electroencephalography and Electromyography as a Non-Invasive Biomarker of Neural Regeneration: A Review of Central and Peripheral Nervous System Injury and Regeneration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.01767)
*Maryam Kheyrollah,Reza Khanbabaie,Chris Ullrich,Mohammad Moulaeifard*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文综述了脑电图（EEG）和肌电图（EMG）作为实时、无创生物标志物在监测中枢神经系统（CNS）和周围神经系统（PNS）损伤及再生中的应用潜力，提出了EEG与EMG联合监测的双系统视角。

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Motivation: 神经系统损伤后再生是一个重要的治疗目标，尤其在中枢神经系统中再生受到限制。虽然结构和分子机制已被充分理解，但能够无创实时监测再生的功能性生物标志物仍然有限。

Method: 通过对比CNS和PNS损伤的生物学与电生理学指标，综述EEG（包括振荡功率、连通性和诱发电位变化）和EMG在监测神经损伤与再生中的作用。

Result: 在CNS损伤中，EEG通常表现为全局性慢波、半球间连贯性中断以及高频部分恢复；在PNS损伤中，EEG可捕捉皮层重塑和体感诱发电位的恢复。EMG则可监测神经再支配和功能性运动输出的恢复。

Conclusion: EEG和EMG不仅是诊断工具，还可作为神经再生的功能性生物标志物，从而连接电生理学、可塑性与临床恢复。

Original Abstract: Regeneration of the nervous system after injury remains an important therapeutic objective, especially in the central nervous system (CNS), in which regeneration is restricted by both neuronal limitations as well as adverse extracellular environments. Conversely, the peripheral nervous system (PNS) displays enhanced regenerative capability in the presence of supportive Schwann cells (SC) and pro-growth stimuli. While the structure and molecular mechanisms are thoroughly understood, functional biomarkers that can non-invasively monitor regeneration in real time are limited. In this review, we discuss the promise of electroencephalography (EEG) as well as electromyography (EMG) as real-time, non-invasive biomarkers to monitor damage to nerves and regeneration in both CNS and PNS contexts.
  First, we contrast biological and electrophysiological indicators of CNS/PNS injury, showing how EEG signs, including oscillatory power, connectivity, and evoked potential changes, reflect dysfunction due to injury as well as neuroplastic reorganization. Also, EMG provides direct insight into muscle activation and peripheral output, providing useful EEG complementation in neuromuscular pathway integrity and reactivation. In CNS injuries (e.g., stroke, spinal cord injury (SCI)), EEG typically shows global slowing, disrupted interhemispheric coherence, and partial recovery of higher frequencies. For PNS injuries, EEG can capture cortical remapping and return of somatosensory evoked responses with re-establishment of the peripheries' connectivity. EMG, in turn, enables monitoring of reinnervation and restoration of functional motor output.
  This review presents a dual-system perspective, positioning EEG and EMG not only as diagnostic tools but also as functional biomarkers of neural regeneration, thereby bridging electrophysiology, plasticity, and clinical recovery.

中文摘要翻译: 神经系统损伤后的再生仍然是一个重要的治疗目标，尤其是在中枢神经系统中，其再生受到神经元内在局限性和不利的细胞外环境的双重限制。相反，周围神经系统在支持性施万细胞和促生长刺激的存在下表现出更强的再生能力。尽管其结构和分子机制已被充分理解，但能够无创实时监测再生的功能性生物标志物仍然有限。在本文中，我们讨论了脑电图（EEG）和肌电图（EMG）作为实时、无创生物标志物在监测中枢和周围神经系统损伤及再生中的潜力。首先，我们对比了CNS/PNS损伤的生物学和电生理学指标，展示了EEG信号（包括振荡功率、连通性和诱发电位变化）如何反映损伤导致的功能障碍以及神经可塑性重组。同时，EMG提供了对肌肉激活和周围输出的直接洞察，在神经肌肉通路完整性和再激活方面提供了有用的EEG补充。在CNS损伤（如卒中、脊髓损伤）中，EEG通常表现为全局性慢波、半球间连贯性中断以及高频部分的恢复。对于PNS损伤，EEG可以捕捉皮层重塑和体感诱发电位随着周围神经连接重建而恢复的过程。而EMG则能够监测神经再支配和功能性运动输出的恢复。本文提出了一个双系统视角，将EEG和EMG不仅定位为诊断工具，而且定位为神经再生的功能性生物标志物，从而架起了电生理学、可塑性和临床恢复之间的桥梁。

</details>
